\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00021}00021 \textcolor{keyword}{SUBROUTINE }cbesh(z, fnu, kode, m, n, cy, nz, ierr)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00022}00022 \textcolor{comment}{!***BEGIN PROLOGUE  CBESH}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00023}00023 \textcolor{comment}{!***DATE WRITTEN   830501   (YYMMDD)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00024}00024 \textcolor{comment}{!***REVISION DATE  890801, 930101   (YYMMDD)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00025}00025 \textcolor{comment}{!***CATEGORY NO.  B5K}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00026}00026 \textcolor{comment}{!***KEYWORDS  H-\/BESSEL FUNCTIONS,BESSEL FUNCTIONS OF COMPLEX ARGUMENT,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00027}00027 \textcolor{comment}{!             BESSEL FUNCTIONS OF THIRD KIND,HANKEL FUNCTIONS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00028}00028 \textcolor{comment}{!***AUTHOR  AMOS, DONALD E., SANDIA NATIONAL LABORATORIES}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00029}00029 \textcolor{comment}{!***PURPOSE  TO COMPUTE THE H-\/BESSEL FUNCTIONS OF A COMPLEX ARGUMENT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00030}00030 \textcolor{comment}{!***DESCRIPTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00031}00031 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00032}00032 \textcolor{comment}{!   ON KODE=1, CBESH COMPUTES AN N MEMBER SEQUENCE OF COMPLEX}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00033}00033 \textcolor{comment}{!   HANKEL (BESSEL) FUNCTIONS CY(J)=H(M,FNU+J-\/1,Z) FOR KINDS M=1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00034}00034 \textcolor{comment}{!   OR 2, REAL, NONNEGATIVE ORDERS FNU+J-\/1, J=1,...,N, AND COMPLEX}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00035}00035 \textcolor{comment}{!   Z.NE.CMPLX(0.0E0,0.0E0) IN THE CUT PLANE -\/PI < ARG(Z) <= PI.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00036}00036 \textcolor{comment}{!   ON KODE=2, CBESH COMPUTES THE SCALED HANKEL FUNCTIONS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00037}00037 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00038}00038 \textcolor{comment}{!   CY(I)=H(M,FNU+J-\/1,Z)*EXP(-\/MM*Z*I)       MM=3-\/2M,      I**2=-\/1.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00039}00039 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00040}00040 \textcolor{comment}{!   WHICH REMOVES THE EXPONENTIAL BEHAVIOR IN BOTH THE UPPER}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00041}00041 \textcolor{comment}{!   AND LOWER HALF PLANES.  DEFINITIONS AND NOTATION ARE FOUND IN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00042}00042 \textcolor{comment}{!   THE NBS HANDBOOK OF MATHEMATICAL FUNCTIONS (REF. 1).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00043}00043 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00044}00044 \textcolor{comment}{!   INPUT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00045}00045 \textcolor{comment}{!     Z      -\/ Z=CMPLX(X,Y), Z.NE.CMPLX(0.,0.),-\/PI < ARG(Z) <= PI}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00046}00046 \textcolor{comment}{!     FNU    -\/ ORDER OF INITIAL H FUNCTION, FNU >= 0.0E0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00047}00047 \textcolor{comment}{!     KODE   -\/ A PARAMETER TO INDICATE THE SCALING OPTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00048}00048 \textcolor{comment}{!              KODE= 1  RETURNS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00049}00049 \textcolor{comment}{!                       CY(J)=H(M,FNU+J-\/1,Z),      J=1,...,N}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00050}00050 \textcolor{comment}{!                  = 2  RETURNS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00051}00051 \textcolor{comment}{!                       CY(J)=H(M,FNU+J-\/1,Z)*EXP(-\/I*Z*(3-\/2M))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00052}00052 \textcolor{comment}{!                            J=1,...,N  ,  I**2=-\/1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00053}00053 \textcolor{comment}{!     M      -\/ KIND OF HANKEL FUNCTION, M=1 OR 2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00054}00054 \textcolor{comment}{!     N      -\/ NUMBER OF MEMBERS OF THE SEQUENCE, N >= 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00055}00055 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00056}00056 \textcolor{comment}{!   OUTPUT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00057}00057 \textcolor{comment}{!     CY     -\/ A COMPLEX VECTOR WHOSE FIRST N COMPONENTS CONTAIN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00058}00058 \textcolor{comment}{!              VALUES FOR THE SEQUENCE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00059}00059 \textcolor{comment}{!              CY(J)=H(M,FNU+J-\/1,Z)  OR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00060}00060 \textcolor{comment}{!              CY(J)=H(M,FNU+J-\/1,Z)*EXP(-\/I*Z*(3-\/2M))  J=1,...,N}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00061}00061 \textcolor{comment}{!              DEPENDING ON KODE, I**2=-\/1.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00062}00062 \textcolor{comment}{!     NZ     -\/ NUMBER OF COMPONENTS SET TO ZERO DUE TO UNDERFLOW,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00063}00063 \textcolor{comment}{!              NZ= 0   , NORMAL RETURN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00064}00064 \textcolor{comment}{!              NZ > 0 , FIRST NZ COMPONENTS OF CY SET TO ZERO DUE TO UNDERFLOW,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00065}00065 \textcolor{comment}{!                        CY(J)=CMPLX(0.0,0.0) J=1,...,NZ WHEN Y > 0.0 AND M=1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00066}00066 \textcolor{comment}{!                        OR Y < 0.0 AND M=2. FOR THE COMPLEMENTARY HALF PLANES,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00067}00067 \textcolor{comment}{!                        NZ STATES ONLY THE NUMBER OF UNDERFLOWS.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00068}00068 \textcolor{comment}{!     IERR    -\/ERROR FLAG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00069}00069 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=0, NORMAL RETURN -\/ COMPUTATION COMPLETED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00070}00070 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=1, INPUT ERROR   -\/ NO COMPUTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00071}00071 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=2, OVERFLOW      -\/ NO COMPUTATION, FNU+N-\/1 TOO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00072}00072 \textcolor{comment}{!                      LARGE OR ABS(Z) TOO SMALL OR BOTH}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00073}00073 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=3, ABS(Z) OR FNU+N-\/1 LARGE -\/ COMPUTATION DONE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00074}00074 \textcolor{comment}{!                      BUT LOSSES OF SIGNIFICANCE BY ARGUMENT REDUCTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00075}00075 \textcolor{comment}{!                      PRODUCE LESS THAN HALF OF MACHINE ACCURACY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00076}00076 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=4, ABS(Z) OR FNU+N-\/1 TOO LARGE -\/ NO COMPUTATION BECAUSE OF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00077}00077 \textcolor{comment}{!                      COMPLETE LOSSES OF SIGNIFICANCE BY ARGUMENT REDUCTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00078}00078 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=5, ERROR              -\/ NO COMPUTATION,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00079}00079 \textcolor{comment}{!                      ALGORITHM TERMINATION CONDITION NOT MET}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00080}00080 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00081}00081 \textcolor{comment}{!***LONG DESCRIPTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00082}00082 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00083}00083 \textcolor{comment}{!    THE COMPUTATION IS CARRIED OUT BY THE RELATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00084}00084 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00085}00085 \textcolor{comment}{!    H(M,FNU,Z)=(1/MP)*EXP(-\/MP*FNU)*K(FNU,Z*EXP(-\/MP))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00086}00086 \textcolor{comment}{!        MP=MM*HPI*I,  MM=3-\/2*M,  HPI=PI/2,  I**2=-\/1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00087}00087 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00088}00088 \textcolor{comment}{!    FOR M=1 OR 2 WHERE THE K BESSEL FUNCTION IS COMPUTED FOR THE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00089}00089 \textcolor{comment}{!    RIGHT HALF PLANE RE(Z) >= 0.0. THE K FUNCTION IS CONTINUED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00090}00090 \textcolor{comment}{!    TO THE LEFT HALF PLANE BY THE RELATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00091}00091 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00092}00092 \textcolor{comment}{!    K(FNU,Z*EXP(MP)) = EXP(-\/MP*FNU)*K(FNU,Z)-\/MP*I(FNU,Z)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00093}00093 \textcolor{comment}{!    MP=MR*PI*I, MR=+1 OR -\/1, RE(Z) > 0, I**2=-\/1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00094}00094 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00095}00095 \textcolor{comment}{!    WHERE I(FNU,Z) IS THE I BESSEL FUNCTION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00096}00096 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00097}00097 \textcolor{comment}{!    EXPONENTIAL DECAY OF H(M,FNU,Z) OCCURS IN THE UPPER HALF Z PLANE FOR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00098}00098 \textcolor{comment}{!    M=1 AND THE LOWER HALF Z PLANE FOR M=2.  EXPONENTIAL GROWTH OCCURS IN THE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00099}00099 \textcolor{comment}{!    COMPLEMENTARY HALF PLANES.  SCALING BY EXP(-\/MM*Z*I) REMOVES THE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00100}00100 \textcolor{comment}{!    EXPONENTIAL BEHAVIOR IN THE WHOLE Z PLANE FOR Z TO INFINITY.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00101}00101 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00102}00102 \textcolor{comment}{!    FOR NEGATIVE ORDERS,THE FORMULAE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00103}00103 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00104}00104 \textcolor{comment}{!          H(1,-\/FNU,Z) = H(1,FNU,Z)*EXP( PI*FNU*I)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00105}00105 \textcolor{comment}{!          H(2,-\/FNU,Z) = H(2,FNU,Z)*EXP(-\/PI*FNU*I)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00106}00106 \textcolor{comment}{!                    I**2=-\/1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00107}00107 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00108}00108 \textcolor{comment}{!    CAN BE USED.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00109}00109 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00110}00110 \textcolor{comment}{!    IN MOST COMPLEX VARIABLE COMPUTATION, ONE MUST EVALUATE ELEMENTARY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00111}00111 \textcolor{comment}{!    FUNCTIONS. WHEN THE MAGNITUDE OF Z OR FNU+N-\/1 IS LARGE, LOSSES OF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00112}00112 \textcolor{comment}{!    SIGNIFICANCE BY ARGUMENT REDUCTION OCCUR.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00113}00113 \textcolor{comment}{!    CONSEQUENTLY, IF EITHER ONE EXCEEDS U1=SQRT(0.5/UR), THEN LOSSES}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00114}00114 \textcolor{comment}{!    EXCEEDING HALF PRECISION ARE LIKELY AND AN ERROR FLAG IERR=3 IS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00115}00115 \textcolor{comment}{!    TRIGGERED WHERE UR=R1MACH(4)=UNIT ROUNDOFF.  ALSO IF EITHER IS LARGER}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00116}00116 \textcolor{comment}{!    THAN U2=0.5/UR, THEN ALL SIGNIFICANCE IS LOST AND IERR=4.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00117}00117 \textcolor{comment}{!    IN ORDER TO USE THE INT FUNCTION, ARGUMENTS MUST BE FURTHER RESTRICTED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00118}00118 \textcolor{comment}{!    NOT TO EXCEED THE LARGEST MACHINE INTEGER, U3=I1MACH(9).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00119}00119 \textcolor{comment}{!    THUS, THE MAGNITUDE OF Z AND FNU+N-\/1 IS RESTRICTED BY MIN(U2,U3).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00120}00120 \textcolor{comment}{!    ON 32 BIT MACHINES, U1,U2, AND U3 ARE APPROXIMATELY 2.0E+3, 4.2E+6,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00121}00121 \textcolor{comment}{!    2.1E+9 IN SINGLE PRECISION ARITHMETIC AND 1.3E+8, 1.8D+16, 2.1E+9 IN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00122}00122 \textcolor{comment}{!    DOUBLE PRECISION ARITHMETIC RESPECTIVELY.  THIS MAKES U2 AND U3}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00123}00123 \textcolor{comment}{!    LIMITING IN THEIR RESPECTIVE ARITHMETICS.  THIS MEANS THAT ONE CAN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00124}00124 \textcolor{comment}{!    EXPECT TO RETAIN, IN THE WORST CASES ON 32 BIT MACHINES, NO DIGITS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00125}00125 \textcolor{comment}{!    IN SINGLE AND ONLY 7 DIGITS IN DOUBLE PRECISION ARITHMETIC.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00126}00126 \textcolor{comment}{!    SIMILAR CONSIDERATIONS HOLD FOR OTHER MACHINES.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00127}00127 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00128}00128 \textcolor{comment}{!    THE APPROXIMATE RELATIVE ERROR IN THE MAGNITUDE OF A COMPLEX BESSEL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00129}00129 \textcolor{comment}{!    FUNCTION CAN BE EXPRESSED BY P*10**S WHERE P=MAX(UNIT ROUNDOFF,1.0E-\/18)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00130}00130 \textcolor{comment}{!    IS THE NOMINAL PRECISION AND 10**S REPRESENTS THE INCREASE IN ERROR DUE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00131}00131 \textcolor{comment}{!    TO ARGUMENT REDUCTION IN THE ELEMENTARY FUNCTIONS.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00132}00132 \textcolor{comment}{!    HERE, S=MAX(1, ABS(LOG10(ABS(Z))), ABS(LOG10(FNU))) APPROXIMATELY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00133}00133 \textcolor{comment}{!    (I.E. S=MAX(1,ABS(EXPONENT OF ABS(Z),ABS(EXPONENT OF FNU)) ).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00134}00134 \textcolor{comment}{!    HOWEVER, THE PHASE ANGLE MAY HAVE ONLY ABSOLUTE ACCURACY.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00135}00135 \textcolor{comment}{!    THIS IS MOST LIKELY TO OCCUR WHEN ONE COMPONENT (IN ABSOLUTE VALUE)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00136}00136 \textcolor{comment}{!    IS LARGER THAN THE OTHER BY SEVERAL ORDERS OF MAGNITUDE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00137}00137 \textcolor{comment}{!    IF ONE COMPONENT IS 10**K LARGER THAN THE OTHER, THEN ONE CAN EXPECT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00138}00138 \textcolor{comment}{!    ONLY MAX(ABS(LOG10(P))-\/K, 0) SIGNIFICANT DIGITS; OR, STATED ANOTHER}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00139}00139 \textcolor{comment}{!    WAY, WHEN K EXCEEDS THE EXPONENT OF P, NO SIGNIFICANT DIGITS REMAIN IN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00140}00140 \textcolor{comment}{!    THE SMALLER COMPONENT.  HOWEVER, THE PHASE ANGLE RETAINS ABSOLUTE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00141}00141 \textcolor{comment}{!    ACCURACY BECAUSE, IN COMPLEX ARITHMETIC WITH PRECISION P, THE SMALLER}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00142}00142 \textcolor{comment}{!    COMPONENT WILL NOT (AS A RULE) DECREASE BELOW P TIMES THE MAGNITUDE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00143}00143 \textcolor{comment}{!    OF THE LARGER COMPONENT.  IN THESE EXTREME CASES, THE PRINCIPAL PHASE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00144}00144 \textcolor{comment}{!    ANGLE IS ON THE ORDER OF +P, -\/P, PI/2-\/P, OR -\/PI/2+P.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00145}00145 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00146}00146 \textcolor{comment}{!***REFERENCES  HANDBOOK OF MATHEMATICAL FUNCTIONS BY M. ABRAMOWITZ AND}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00147}00147 \textcolor{comment}{!        I. A. STEGUN, NBS AMS SERIES 55, U.S. DEPT. OF COMMERCE, 1955.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00194}00194 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00195}00195 \textcolor{comment}{!     SET PARAMETERS RELATED TO MACHINE CONSTANTS.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00196}00196 \textcolor{comment}{!     TOL IS THE APPROXIMATE UNIT ROUNDOFF LIMITED TO 1.0E-\/18.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00197}00197 \textcolor{comment}{!     ELIM IS THE APPROXIMATE EXPONENTIAL OVER-\/ AND UNDERFLOW LIMIT.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00198}00198 \textcolor{comment}{!     EXP(-\/ELIM) < EXP(-\/ALIM)=EXP(-\/ELIM)/TOL    AND}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00199}00199 \textcolor{comment}{!     EXP(ELIM) > EXP(ALIM)=EXP(ELIM)*TOL       ARE INTERVALS NEAR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00200}00200 \textcolor{comment}{!     UNDERFLOW AND OVERFLOW LIMITS WHERE SCALED ARITHMETIC IS DONE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00201}00201 \textcolor{comment}{!     RL IS THE LOWER BOUNDARY OF THE ASYMPTOTIC EXPANSION FOR LARGE Z.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00202}00202 \textcolor{comment}{!     DIG = NUMBER OF BASE 10 DIGITS IN TOL = 10**(-\/DIG).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00203}00203 \textcolor{comment}{!     FNUL IS THE LOWER BOUNDARY OF THE ASYMPTOTIC SERIES FOR LARGE FNU}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00204}00204 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00205}00205 tol = max(epsilon(0.0\_dp), 1.0d-\/18)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00206}00206 k1 = minexponent(0.0\_dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00207}00207 k2 = maxexponent(0.0\_dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00208}00208 r1m5 = log10( real( radix(0.0\_dp), kind=dp) )}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00209}00209 k = min(abs(k1), abs(k2))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00210}00210 elim = 2.303\_dp * (k*r1m5 -\/ 3.0\_dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00211}00211 k1 = digits(0.0\_dp) -\/ 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00212}00212 aa = r1m5 * k1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00213}00213 dig = min(aa, 18.0\_dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00214}00214 aa = aa * 2.303\_dp}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00215}00215 alim = elim + max(-\/aa, -\/41.45\_dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00216}00216 fnul = 10.0\_dp + 6.0\_dp * (dig -\/ 3.0\_dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00217}00217 rl = 1.2\_dp * dig + 3.0\_dp}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00218}00218 fn = fnu + (nn-\/1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00219}00219 mm = 3 -\/ m -\/ m}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00220}00220 fmm = mm}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00221}00221 zn = z * cmplx(0.0\_dp, -\/fmm, kind=dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00222}00222 xn = real(zn, kind=dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00223}00223 yn = aimag(zn)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00224}00224 az = abs(z)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00225}00225 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00226}00226 \textcolor{comment}{!     TEST FOR RANGE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00227}00227 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00292}00292 \textcolor{comment}{!     H(M,FNU,Z) = -\/FMM*(I/HPI)*(ZT**FNU)*K(FNU,-\/Z*ZT)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00293}00293 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00294}00294 \textcolor{comment}{!     ZT=EXP(-\/FMM*HPI*I) = CMPLX(0.0,-\/FMM), FMM=3-\/2*M, M=1,2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00295}00295 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00296}00296       20 sgn = sign(hpi,-\/fmm)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00297}00297 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00298}00298 \textcolor{comment}{!     CALCULATE EXP(FNU*HPI*I) TO MINIMIZE LOSSES OF SIGNIFICANCE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00299}00299 \textcolor{comment}{!     WHEN FNU IS LARGE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00300}00300 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00301}00301       inu = fnu}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00302}00302       inuh = inu / 2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00303}00303       ir = inu -\/ 2 * inuh}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00304}00304       arg = (fnu -\/ (inu-\/ir)) * sgn}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00305}00305       rhpi = 1.0\_dp / sgn}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00306}00306       cpn = rhpi * cos(arg)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00307}00307       spn = rhpi * sin(arg)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00308}00308 \textcolor{comment}{!     ZN = CMPLX(-\/SPN,CPN)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00309}00309       csgn = cmplx(-\/spn, cpn, kind=dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00310}00310 \textcolor{comment}{!     IF (MOD(INUH,2).EQ.1) ZN = -\/ZN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00311}00311       \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (mod(inuh,2) == 1) csgn = -\/csgn}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00312}00312       zt = cmplx(0.0\_dp, -\/fmm, kind=dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00313}00313       rtol = 1.0\_dp / tol}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00314}00314       ascle = ufl * rtol}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00315}00315       \textcolor{keywordflow}{DO}  i = 1, nn}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00316}00316 \textcolor{comment}{!       CY(I) = CY(I)*ZN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00317}00317 \textcolor{comment}{!       ZN = ZN*ZT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00318}00318         zn = cy(i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00319}00319         aa = real(zn, kind=dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00320}00320         bb = aimag(zn)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00321}00321         atol = 1.0\_dp}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00322}00322         \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (max(abs(aa),abs(bb)) <= ascle) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00323}00323           zn = zn * rtol}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00324}00324           atol = tol}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00325}00325 \textcolor{keywordflow}{        END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00326}00326         zn = zn * csgn}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00327}00327         cy(i) = zn * atol}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00328}00328         csgn = csgn * zt}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00329}00329 \textcolor{keywordflow}{      END DO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00330}00330       \textcolor{keywordflow}{RETURN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00331}00331 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00332}00332       40 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (xn >= 0.0\_dp) \textcolor{keywordflow}{RETURN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00333}00333 \textcolor{keywordflow}{    END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00334}00334 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00335}00335     50 ierr = 2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00336}00336     nz = 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00337}00337     \textcolor{keywordflow}{RETURN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00338}00338 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00340}00340     nz = 0}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00342}00342     \textcolor{keywordflow}{RETURN}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00352}00352 \textcolor{keyword}{SUBROUTINE }cbesi(z, fnu, kode, n, cy, nz, ierr)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00353}00353 \textcolor{comment}{!***BEGIN PROLOGUE  CBESI}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00354}00354 \textcolor{comment}{!***DATE WRITTEN   830501   (YYMMDD)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00355}00355 \textcolor{comment}{!***REVISION DATE  890801, 930101   (YYMMDD)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00356}00356 \textcolor{comment}{!***CATEGORY NO.  B5K}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00357}00357 \textcolor{comment}{!***KEYWORDS  I-\/BESSEL FUNCTION,COMPLEX BESSEL FUNCTION,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00358}00358 \textcolor{comment}{!             MODIFIED BESSEL FUNCTION OF THE FIRST KIND}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00359}00359 \textcolor{comment}{!***AUTHOR  AMOS, DONALD E., SANDIA NATIONAL LABORATORIES}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00360}00360 \textcolor{comment}{!***PURPOSE  TO COMPUTE I-\/BESSEL FUNCTIONS OF COMPLEX ARGUMENT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00361}00361 \textcolor{comment}{!***DESCRIPTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00362}00362 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00363}00363 \textcolor{comment}{!   ON KODE=1, CBESI COMPUTES AN N MEMBER SEQUENCE OF COMPLEX}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00364}00364 \textcolor{comment}{!   BESSEL FUNCTIONS CY(J)=I(FNU+J-\/1,Z) FOR REAL (dp), NONNEGATIVE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00365}00365 \textcolor{comment}{!   ORDERS FNU+J-\/1, J=1,...,N AND COMPLEX Z IN THE CUT PLANE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00366}00366 \textcolor{comment}{!   -\/PI < ARG(Z) <= PI. ON KODE=2, CBESI RETURNS THE SCALED FUNCTIONS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00367}00367 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00368}00368 \textcolor{comment}{!   CY(J)=EXP(-\/ABS(X))*I(FNU+J-\/1,Z)   J = 1,...,N , X=REAL(Z)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00369}00369 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00370}00370 \textcolor{comment}{!   WITH THE EXPONENTIAL GROWTH REMOVED IN BOTH THE LEFT AND}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00371}00371 \textcolor{comment}{!   RIGHT HALF PLANES FOR Z TO INFINITY. DEFINITIONS AND}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00372}00372 \textcolor{comment}{!   NOTATION ARE FOUND IN THE NBS HANDBOOK OF MATHEMATICAL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00373}00373 \textcolor{comment}{!   FUNCTIONS (REF.1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00374}00374 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00375}00375 \textcolor{comment}{!   INPUT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00376}00376 \textcolor{comment}{!     Z      -\/ Z=CMPLX(X,Y),  -\/PI < ARG(Z) <= PI}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00377}00377 \textcolor{comment}{!     FNU    -\/ ORDER OF INITIAL I FUNCTION, FNU >= 0.0\_dp}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00378}00378 \textcolor{comment}{!     KODE   -\/ A PARAMETER TO INDICATE THE SCALING OPTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00379}00379 \textcolor{comment}{!              KODE= 1  RETURNS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00380}00380 \textcolor{comment}{!                       CY(J)=I(FNU+J-\/1,Z), J=1,...,N}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00381}00381 \textcolor{comment}{!                  = 2  RETURNS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00382}00382 \textcolor{comment}{!                       CY(J)=I(FNU+J-\/1,Z)*EXP(-\/ABS(X)), J=1,...,N}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00383}00383 \textcolor{comment}{!     N      -\/ NUMBER OF MEMBERS OF THE SEQUENCE, N >= 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00384}00384 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00385}00385 \textcolor{comment}{!   OUTPUT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00386}00386 \textcolor{comment}{!     CY     -\/ A COMPLEX VECTOR WHOSE FIRST N COMPONENTS CONTAIN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00387}00387 \textcolor{comment}{!              VALUES FOR THE SEQUENCE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00388}00388 \textcolor{comment}{!              CY(J)=I(FNU+J-\/1,Z)  OR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00389}00389 \textcolor{comment}{!              CY(J)=I(FNU+J-\/1,Z)*EXP(-\/ABS(X))  J=1,...,N}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00390}00390 \textcolor{comment}{!              DEPENDING ON KODE, X=REAL(Z)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00391}00391 \textcolor{comment}{!     NZ     -\/ NUMBER OF COMPONENTS SET TO ZERO DUE TO UNDERFLOW,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00392}00392 \textcolor{comment}{!              NZ= 0   , NORMAL RETURN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00393}00393 \textcolor{comment}{!              NZ > 0 , LAST NZ COMPONENTS OF CY SET TO ZERO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00394}00394 \textcolor{comment}{!                        DUE TO UNDERFLOW, CY(J)=CMPLX(0.0,0.0),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00395}00395 \textcolor{comment}{!                        J = N-\/NZ+1,...,N}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00396}00396 \textcolor{comment}{!     IERR   -\/ ERROR FLAG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00397}00397 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=0, NORMAL RETURN -\/ COMPUTATION COMPLETED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00398}00398 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=1, INPUT ERROR   -\/ NO COMPUTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00399}00399 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=2, OVERFLOW      -\/ NO COMPUTATION, REAL(Z) TOO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00400}00400 \textcolor{comment}{!                      LARGE ON KODE=1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00401}00401 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=3, ABS(Z) OR FNU+N-\/1 LARGE -\/ COMPUTATION DONE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00402}00402 \textcolor{comment}{!                      BUT LOSSES OF SIGNIFICANCE BY ARGUMENT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00403}00403 \textcolor{comment}{!                      REDUCTION PRODUCE LESS THAN HALF OF MACHINE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00404}00404 \textcolor{comment}{!                      ACCURACY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00405}00405 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=4, ABS(Z) OR FNU+N-\/1 TOO LARGE -\/ NO COMPUTA-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00406}00406 \textcolor{comment}{!                      TION BECAUSE OF COMPLETE LOSSES OF SIGNIFI-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00407}00407 \textcolor{comment}{!                      CANCE BY ARGUMENT REDUCTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00408}00408 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=5, ERROR              -\/ NO COMPUTATION,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00409}00409 \textcolor{comment}{!                      ALGORITHM TERMINATION CONDITION NOT MET}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00410}00410 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00411}00411 \textcolor{comment}{!***LONG DESCRIPTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00412}00412 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00413}00413 \textcolor{comment}{!   THE COMPUTATION IS CARRIED OUT BY THE POWER SERIES FOR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00414}00414 \textcolor{comment}{!   SMALL ABS(Z), THE ASYMPTOTIC EXPANSION FOR LARGE ABS(Z),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00415}00415 \textcolor{comment}{!   THE MILLER ALGORITHM NORMALIZED BY THE WRONSKIAN AND A}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00416}00416 \textcolor{comment}{!   NEUMANN SERIES FOR IMTERMEDIATE MAGNITUDES, AND THE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00417}00417 \textcolor{comment}{!   UNIFORM ASYMPTOTIC EXPANSIONS FOR I(FNU,Z) AND J(FNU,Z)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00418}00418 \textcolor{comment}{!   FOR LARGE ORDERS. BACKWARD RECURRENCE IS USED TO GENERATE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00419}00419 \textcolor{comment}{!   SEQUENCES OR REDUCE ORDERS WHEN NECESSARY.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00420}00420 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00421}00421 \textcolor{comment}{!   THE CALCULATIONS ABOVE ARE DONE IN THE RIGHT HALF PLANE AND}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00422}00422 \textcolor{comment}{!   CONTINUED INTO THE LEFT HALF PLANE BY THE FORMULA}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00423}00423 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00424}00424 \textcolor{comment}{!   I(FNU,Z*EXP(M*PI)) = EXP(M*PI*FNU)*I(FNU,Z)  REAL(Z) > 0.0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00425}00425 \textcolor{comment}{!                 M = +I OR -\/I,  I**2=-\/1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00426}00426 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00427}00427 \textcolor{comment}{!   FOR NEGATIVE ORDERS,THE FORMULA}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00428}00428 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00429}00429 \textcolor{comment}{!        I(-\/FNU,Z) = I(FNU,Z) + (2/PI)*SIN(PI*FNU)*K(FNU,Z)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00430}00430 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00431}00431 \textcolor{comment}{!   CAN BE USED.  HOWEVER,FOR LARGE ORDERS CLOSE TO INTEGERS, THE FUNCTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00432}00432 \textcolor{comment}{!   CHANGES RADICALLY.  WHEN FNU IS A LARGE POSITIVE INTEGER,THE MAGNITUDE OF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00433}00433 \textcolor{comment}{!   I(-\/FNU,Z) = I(FNU,Z) IS A LARGE NEGATIVE POWER OF TEN.  BUT WHEN FNU IS NOT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00434}00434 \textcolor{comment}{!   AN INTEGER, K(FNU,Z) DOMINATES IN MAGNITUDE WITH A LARGE POSITIVE POWER OF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00435}00435 \textcolor{comment}{!   TEN AND THE MOST THAT THE SECOND TERM CAN BE REDUCED IS BY UNIT ROUNDOFF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00436}00436 \textcolor{comment}{!   FROM THE COEFFICIENT. THUS, WIDE CHANGES CAN OCCUR WITHIN UNIT ROUNDOFF OF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00437}00437 \textcolor{comment}{!   A LARGE INTEGER FOR FNU.  HERE, LARGE MEANS FNU > ABS(Z).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00438}00438 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00439}00439 \textcolor{comment}{!   IN MOST COMPLEX VARIABLE COMPUTATION, ONE MUST EVALUATE ELEMENTARY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00440}00440 \textcolor{comment}{!   FUNCTIONS.  WHEN THE MAGNITUDE OF Z OR FNU+N-\/1 IS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00441}00441 \textcolor{comment}{!   LARGE, LOSSES OF SIGNIFICANCE BY ARGUMENT REDUCTION OCCUR.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00442}00442 \textcolor{comment}{!   CONSEQUENTLY, IF EITHER ONE EXCEEDS U1=SQRT(0.5/UR), THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00443}00443 \textcolor{comment}{!   LOSSES EXCEEDING HALF PRECISION ARE LIKELY AND AN ERROR FLAG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00444}00444 \textcolor{comment}{!   IERR=3 IS TRIGGERED WHERE UR=EPSILON(0.0\_dp)=UNIT ROUNDOFF.  ALSO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00445}00445 \textcolor{comment}{!   IF EITHER IS LARGER THAN U2=0.5/UR, THEN ALL SIGNIFICANCE IS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00446}00446 \textcolor{comment}{!   LOST AND IERR=4. IN ORDER TO USE THE INT FUNCTION, ARGUMENTS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00447}00447 \textcolor{comment}{!   MUST BE FURTHER RESTRICTED NOT TO EXCEED THE LARGEST MACHINE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00448}00448 \textcolor{comment}{!   INTEGER, U3=HUGE(0). THUS, THE MAGNITUDE OF Z AND FNU+N-\/1 IS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00449}00449 \textcolor{comment}{!   RESTRICTED BY MIN(U2,U3). ON 32 BIT MACHINES, U1,U2, AND U3}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00450}00450 \textcolor{comment}{!   ARE APPROXIMATELY 2.0E+3, 4.2E+6, 2.1E+9 IN SINGLE PRECISION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00451}00451 \textcolor{comment}{!   ARITHMETIC AND 1.3E+8, 1.8D+16, 2.1E+9 IN DOUBLE PRECISION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00452}00452 \textcolor{comment}{!   ARITHMETIC RESPECTIVELY. THIS MAKES U2 AND U3 LIMITING IN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00453}00453 \textcolor{comment}{!   THEIR RESPECTIVE ARITHMETICS. THIS MEANS THAT ONE CAN EXPECT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00454}00454 \textcolor{comment}{!   TO RETAIN, IN THE WORST CASES ON 32 BIT MACHINES, NO DIGITS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00455}00455 \textcolor{comment}{!   IN SINGLE AND ONLY 7 DIGITS IN DOUBLE PRECISION ARITHMETIC.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00456}00456 \textcolor{comment}{!   SIMILAR CONSIDERATIONS HOLD FOR OTHER MACHINES.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00457}00457 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00458}00458 \textcolor{comment}{!   THE APPROXIMATE RELATIVE ERROR IN THE MAGNITUDE OF A COMPLEX BESSEL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00459}00459 \textcolor{comment}{!   FUNCTION CAN BE EXPRESSED BY P*10**S WHERE P = MAX(UNIT ROUNDOFF,1.0E-\/18)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00460}00460 \textcolor{comment}{!   IS THE NOMINAL PRECISION AND 10**S REPRESENTS THE INCREASE IN ERROR DUE TO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00461}00461 \textcolor{comment}{!   ARGUMENT REDUCTION IN THE ELEMENTARY FUNCTIONS.  HERE, S =}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00462}00462 \textcolor{comment}{!   MAX(1,ABS(LOG10(ABS(Z))), ABS(LOG10(FNU))) APPROXIMATELY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00463}00463 \textcolor{comment}{!   (I.E. S = MAX(1,ABS(EXPONENT OF ABS(Z), ABS(EXPONENT OF FNU)) ).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00464}00464 \textcolor{comment}{!   HOWEVER, THE PHASE ANGLE MAY HAVE ONLY ABSOLUTE ACCURACY.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00465}00465 \textcolor{comment}{!   THIS IS MOST LIKELY TO OCCUR WHEN ONE COMPONENT (IN ABSOLUTE VALUE) IS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00466}00466 \textcolor{comment}{!   LARGER THAN THE OTHER BY SEVERAL ORDERS OF MAGNITUDE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00467}00467 \textcolor{comment}{!   IF ONE COMPONENT IS 10**K LARGER THAN THE OTHER, THEN ONE CAN EXPECT ONLY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00468}00468 \textcolor{comment}{!   MAX(ABS(LOG10(P))-\/K, 0) SIGNIFICANT DIGITS; OR, STATED ANOTHER WAY, WHEN K}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00469}00469 \textcolor{comment}{!   EXCEEDS THE EXPONENT OF P, NO SIGNIFICANT DIGITS REMAIN IN THE SMALLER}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00470}00470 \textcolor{comment}{!   COMPONENT.  HOWEVER, THE PHASE ANGLE RETAINS ABSOLUTE ACCURACY BECAUSE,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00471}00471 \textcolor{comment}{!   IN COMPLEX ARITHMETIC WITH PRECISION P, THE SMALLER COMPONENT WILL NOT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00472}00472 \textcolor{comment}{!   (AS A RULE) DECREASE BELOW P TIMES THE MAGNITUDE OF THE LARGER COMPONENT.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00473}00473 \textcolor{comment}{!   IN THESE EXTREME CASES, THE PRINCIPAL PHASE ANGLE IS ON THE ORDER OF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00474}00474 \textcolor{comment}{!   +P, -\/P, PI/2-\/P, OR -\/PI/2+P.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00475}00475 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00580}00580       \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (nn == 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{RETURN}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00583}00583       \textcolor{keywordflow}{DO}  i = 1, nn}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00584}00584 \textcolor{comment}{!       CY(I) = CY(I)*CSGN}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00592}00592 \textcolor{keywordflow}{        END IF}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00594}00594         cy(i) = zn * atol}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00595}00595         csgn = -\/csgn}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00596}00596 \textcolor{keywordflow}{      END DO}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00602}00602       \textcolor{keywordflow}{RETURN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00603}00603 \textcolor{keywordflow}{    END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00604}00604     nz = 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00605}00605     ierr = 5}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00606}00606     \textcolor{keywordflow}{RETURN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00607}00607 \textcolor{keywordflow}{  END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00608}00608 \textcolor{keywordflow}{END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00609}00609 nz = 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00610}00610 ierr = 4}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00613}00613 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00615}00615 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00616}00616 \textcolor{keyword}{SUBROUTINE }cbesj(z, fnu, kode, n, cy, nz, ierr)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00617}00617 \textcolor{comment}{!***BEGIN PROLOGUE  CBESJ}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00618}00618 \textcolor{comment}{!***DATE WRITTEN   830501   (YYMMDD)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00619}00619 \textcolor{comment}{!***REVISION DATE  890801, 930101   (YYMMDD)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00620}00620 \textcolor{comment}{!***CATEGORY NO.  B5K}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00621}00621 \textcolor{comment}{!***KEYWORDS  J-\/BESSEL FUNCTION,BESSEL FUNCTION OF COMPLEX ARGUMENT,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00622}00622 \textcolor{comment}{!             BESSEL FUNCTION OF FIRST KIND}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00623}00623 \textcolor{comment}{!***AUTHOR  AMOS, DONALD E., SANDIA NATIONAL LABORATORIES}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00624}00624 \textcolor{comment}{!***PURPOSE  TO COMPUTE THE J-\/BESSEL FUNCTION OF A COMPLEX ARGUMENT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00625}00625 \textcolor{comment}{!***DESCRIPTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00626}00626 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00627}00627 \textcolor{comment}{!    ON KODE=1, CBESJ COMPUTES AN N MEMBER  SEQUENCE OF COMPLEX}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00628}00628 \textcolor{comment}{!    BESSEL FUNCTIONS CY(I) = J(FNU+I-\/1,Z) FOR REAL (dp), NONNEGATIVE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00629}00629 \textcolor{comment}{!    ORDERS FNU+I-\/1, I=1,...,N AND COMPLEX Z IN THE CUT PLANE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00630}00630 \textcolor{comment}{!    -\/PI < ARG(Z) <= PI.  ON KODE=2, CBESJ RETURNS THE SCALED FUNCTIONS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00631}00631 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00632}00632 \textcolor{comment}{!    CY(I) = EXP(-\/ABS(Y))*J(FNU+I-\/1,Z)   I = 1,...,N , Y=AIMAG(Z)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00633}00633 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00634}00634 \textcolor{comment}{!    WHICH REMOVE THE EXPONENTIAL GROWTH IN BOTH THE UPPER AND}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00635}00635 \textcolor{comment}{!    LOWER HALF PLANES FOR Z TO INFINITY.  DEFINITIONS AND NOTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00636}00636 \textcolor{comment}{!    ARE FOUND IN THE NBS HANDBOOK OF MATHEMATICAL FUNCTIONS (REF. 1).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00637}00637 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00638}00638 \textcolor{comment}{!    INPUT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00639}00639 \textcolor{comment}{!      Z      -\/ Z=CMPLX(X,Y),  -\/PI < ARG(Z) <= PI}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00640}00640 \textcolor{comment}{!      FNU    -\/ ORDER OF INITIAL J FUNCTION, FNU >= 0.0\_dp}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00641}00641 \textcolor{comment}{!      KODE   -\/ A PARAMETER TO INDICATE THE SCALING OPTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00642}00642 \textcolor{comment}{!               KODE= 1  RETURNS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00643}00643 \textcolor{comment}{!                        CY(I)=J(FNU+I-\/1,Z), I=1,...,N}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00644}00644 \textcolor{comment}{!                   = 2  RETURNS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00645}00645 \textcolor{comment}{!                        CY(I)=J(FNU+I-\/1,Z)*EXP(-\/ABS(Y)), I=1,...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00646}00646 \textcolor{comment}{!      N      -\/ NUMBER OF MEMBERS OF THE SEQUENCE, N >= 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00647}00647 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00648}00648 \textcolor{comment}{!    OUTPUT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00649}00649 \textcolor{comment}{!      CY     -\/ A COMPLEX VECTOR WHOSE FIRST N COMPONENTS CONTAIN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00650}00650 \textcolor{comment}{!               VALUES FOR THE SEQUENCE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00651}00651 \textcolor{comment}{!               CY(I)=J(FNU+I-\/1,Z)  OR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00652}00652 \textcolor{comment}{!               CY(I)=J(FNU+I-\/1,Z)*EXP(-\/ABS(Y))  I=1,...,N}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00653}00653 \textcolor{comment}{!               DEPENDING ON KODE, Y=AIMAG(Z).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00654}00654 \textcolor{comment}{!      NZ     -\/ NUMBER OF COMPONENTS SET TO ZERO DUE TO UNDERFLOW,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00655}00655 \textcolor{comment}{!               NZ= 0   , NORMAL RETURN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00656}00656 \textcolor{comment}{!               NZ > 0 , LAST NZ COMPONENTS OF CY SET TO ZERO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00657}00657 \textcolor{comment}{!                         DUE TO UNDERFLOW, CY(I)=CMPLX(0.0,0.0),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00658}00658 \textcolor{comment}{!                         I = N-\/NZ+1,...,N}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00659}00659 \textcolor{comment}{!      IERR   -\/ ERROR FLAG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00660}00660 \textcolor{comment}{!               IERR=0, NORMAL RETURN -\/ COMPUTATION COMPLETED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00661}00661 \textcolor{comment}{!               IERR=1, INPUT ERROR   -\/ NO COMPUTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00662}00662 \textcolor{comment}{!               IERR=2, OVERFLOW      -\/ NO COMPUTATION, AIMAG(Z)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00663}00663 \textcolor{comment}{!                       TOO LARGE ON KODE=1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00664}00664 \textcolor{comment}{!               IERR=3, ABS(Z) OR FNU+N-\/1 LARGE -\/ COMPUTATION DONE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00665}00665 \textcolor{comment}{!                       BUT LOSSES OF SIGNIFICANCE BY ARGUMENT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00666}00666 \textcolor{comment}{!                       REDUCTION PRODUCE LESS THAN HALF OF MACHINE ACCURACY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00667}00667 \textcolor{comment}{!               IERR=4, ABS(Z) OR FNU+N-\/1 TOO LARGE -\/ NO COMPUTATION BECAUSE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00668}00668 \textcolor{comment}{!                       OF COMPLETE LOSSES OF SIGNIFICANCE BY ARGUMENT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00669}00669 \textcolor{comment}{!                       REDUCTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00670}00670 \textcolor{comment}{!               IERR=5, ERROR              -\/ NO COMPUTATION,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00671}00671 \textcolor{comment}{!                       ALGORITHM TERMINATION CONDITION NOT MET}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00672}00672 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00673}00673 \textcolor{comment}{!***LONG DESCRIPTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00674}00674 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00675}00675 \textcolor{comment}{!    THE COMPUTATION IS CARRIED OUT BY THE FORMULA}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00676}00676 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00677}00677 \textcolor{comment}{!    J(FNU,Z)=EXP( FNU*PI*I/2)*I(FNU,-\/I*Z)    AIMAG(Z) >= 0.0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00678}00678 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00679}00679 \textcolor{comment}{!    J(FNU,Z)=EXP(-\/FNU*PI*I/2)*I(FNU, I*Z)    AIMAG(Z) < 0.0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00680}00680 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00681}00681 \textcolor{comment}{!    WHERE I**2 = -\/1 AND I(FNU,Z) IS THE I BESSEL FUNCTION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00682}00682 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00683}00683 \textcolor{comment}{!    FOR NEGATIVE ORDERS,THE FORMULA}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00684}00684 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00685}00685 \textcolor{comment}{!         J(-\/FNU,Z) = J(FNU,Z)*COS(PI*FNU) -\/ Y(FNU,Z)*SIN(PI*FNU)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00686}00686 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00687}00687 \textcolor{comment}{!    CAN BE USED.  HOWEVER,FOR LARGE ORDERS CLOSE TO INTEGERS, THE FUNCTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00688}00688 \textcolor{comment}{!    CHANGES RADICALLY.  WHEN FNU IS A LARGE POSITIVE INTEGER, THE MAGNITUDE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00689}00689 \textcolor{comment}{!    OF J(-\/FNU,Z)=J(FNU,Z)*COS(PI*FNU) IS A LARGE NEGATIVE POWER OF TEN.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00690}00690 \textcolor{comment}{!    BUT WHEN FNU IS NOT AN INTEGER, Y(FNU,Z) DOMINATES IN MAGNITUDE WITH A}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00691}00691 \textcolor{comment}{!    LARGE POSITIVE POWER OF TEN AND THE MOST THAT THE SECOND TERM CAN BE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00692}00692 \textcolor{comment}{!    REDUCED IS BY UNIT ROUNDOFF FROM THE COEFFICIENT.  THUS, WIDE CHANGES CAN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00693}00693 \textcolor{comment}{!    OCCUR WITHIN UNIT ROUNDOFF OF A LARGE INTEGER FOR FNU.  HERE, LARGE MEANS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00694}00694 \textcolor{comment}{!    FNU > ABS(Z).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00695}00695 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00696}00696 \textcolor{comment}{!    IN MOST COMPLEX VARIABLE COMPUTATION, ONE MUST EVALUATE ELEMENTARY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00697}00697 \textcolor{comment}{!    FUNCTIONS.  WHEN THE MAGNITUDE OF Z OR FNU+N-\/1 IS LARGE, LOSSES OF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00698}00698 \textcolor{comment}{!    SIGNIFICANCE BY ARGUMENT REDUCTION OCCUR.  CONSEQUENTLY, IF EITHER ONE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00699}00699 \textcolor{comment}{!    EXCEEDS U1=SQRT(0.5/UR), THEN LOSSES EXCEEDING HALF PRECISION ARE LIKELY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00700}00700 \textcolor{comment}{!    AND AN ERROR FLAG IERR=3 IS TRIGGERED WHERE UR = EPSILON(0.0\_dp) = UNIT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00701}00701 \textcolor{comment}{!    ROUNDOFF.  ALSO IF EITHER IS LARGER THAN U2=0.5/UR, THEN ALL SIGNIFICANCE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00702}00702 \textcolor{comment}{!    IS LOST AND IERR=4.  IN ORDER TO USE THE INT FUNCTION, ARGUMENTS MUST BE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00703}00703 \textcolor{comment}{!    FURTHER RESTRICTED NOT TO EXCEED THE LARGEST MACHINE INTEGER, U3 = HUGE(0).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00704}00704 \textcolor{comment}{!    THUS, THE MAGNITUDE OF Z AND FNU+N-\/1 IS RESTRICTED BY MIN(U2,U3).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00705}00705 \textcolor{comment}{!    ON 32 BIT MACHINES, U1,U2, AND U3 ARE APPROXIMATELY 2.0E+3, 4.2E+6, 2.1E+9}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00706}00706 \textcolor{comment}{!    IN SINGLE PRECISION ARITHMETIC AND 1.3E+8, 1.8D+16, 2.1E+9 IN DOUBLE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00707}00707 \textcolor{comment}{!    PRECISION ARITHMETIC RESPECTIVELY.  THIS MAKES U2 AND U3 LIMITING IN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00708}00708 \textcolor{comment}{!    THEIR RESPECTIVE ARITHMETICS.  THIS MEANS THAT ONE CAN EXPECT TO RETAIN,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00709}00709 \textcolor{comment}{!    IN THE WORST CASES ON 32 BIT MACHINES, NO DIGITS IN SINGLE AND ONLY 7}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00710}00710 \textcolor{comment}{!    DIGITS IN DOUBLE PRECISION ARITHMETIC.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00711}00711 \textcolor{comment}{!    SIMILAR CONSIDERATIONS HOLD FOR OTHER MACHINES.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00712}00712 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00713}00713 \textcolor{comment}{!    THE APPROXIMATE RELATIVE ERROR IN THE MAGNITUDE OF A COMPLEX BESSEL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00714}00714 \textcolor{comment}{!    FUNCTION CAN BE EXPRESSED BY P*10**S WHERE P = MAX(UNIT ROUNDOFF, 1.0E-\/18)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00715}00715 \textcolor{comment}{!    IS THE NOMINAL PRECISION AND 10**S REPRESENTS THE INCREASE IN ERROR DUE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00716}00716 \textcolor{comment}{!    TO ARGUMENT REDUCTION IN THE ELEMENTARY FUNCTIONS.  HERE,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00717}00717 \textcolor{comment}{!    S = MAX(1,ABS(LOG10(ABS(Z))), ABS(LOG10(FNU))) APPROXIMATELY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00718}00718 \textcolor{comment}{!    (I.E. S = MAX(1, ABS(EXPONENT OF ABS(Z), ABS(EXPONENT OF FNU)) ).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00719}00719 \textcolor{comment}{!    HOWEVER, THE PHASE ANGLE MAY HAVE ONLY ABSOLUTE ACCURACY.  THIS IS MOST}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00720}00720 \textcolor{comment}{!    LIKELY TO OCCUR WHEN ONE COMPONENT (IN ABSOLUTE VALUE) IS LARGER THAN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00721}00721 \textcolor{comment}{!    THE OTHER BY SEVERAL ORDERS OF MAGNITUDE.  IF ONE COMPONENT IS 10**K}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00722}00722 \textcolor{comment}{!    LARGER THAN THE OTHER, THEN ONE CAN EXPECT ONLY MAX(ABS(LOG10(P))-\/K, 0)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00723}00723 \textcolor{comment}{!    SIGNIFICANT DIGITS; OR, STATED ANOTHER WAY, WHEN K EXCEEDS THE EXPONENT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00724}00724 \textcolor{comment}{!    OF P, NO SIGNIFICANT DIGITS REMAIN IN THE SMALLER COMPONENT.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00725}00725 \textcolor{comment}{!    HOWEVER, THE PHASE ANGLE RETAINS ABSOLUTE ACCURACY BECAUSE, IN COMPLEX}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00726}00726 \textcolor{comment}{!    ARITHMETIC WITH PRECISION P, THE SMALLER COMPONENT WILL NOT (AS A RULE)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00727}00727 \textcolor{comment}{!    DECREASE BELOW P TIMES THE MAGNITUDE OF THE LARGER COMPONENT.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00728}00728 \textcolor{comment}{!    IN THESE EXTREME CASES, THE PRINCIPAL PHASE ANGLE IS ON THE ORDER OF +P,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00729}00729 \textcolor{comment}{!    -\/P, PI/2-\/P, OR -\/PI/2+P.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00730}00730 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00731}00731 \textcolor{comment}{!***REFERENCES  HANDBOOK OF MATHEMATICAL FUNCTIONS BY M. ABRAMOWITZ AND}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00732}00732 \textcolor{comment}{!         I. A. STEGUN, NBS AMS SERIES 55, U.S. DEPT. OF COMMERCE, 1955.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00733}00733 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00734}00734 \textcolor{comment}{!       COMPUTATION OF BESSEL FUNCTIONS OF COMPLEX ARGUMENT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00735}00735 \textcolor{comment}{!         BY D. E. AMOS, SAND83-\/0083, MAY 1983.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00736}00736 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00737}00737 \textcolor{comment}{!       COMPUTATION OF BESSEL FUNCTIONS OF COMPLEX ARGUMENT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00738}00738 \textcolor{comment}{!         AND LARGE ORDER BY D. E. AMOS, SAND83-\/0643, MAY 1983}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00739}00739 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00740}00740 \textcolor{comment}{!       A SUBROUTINE PACKAGE FOR BESSEL FUNCTIONS OF A COMPLEX ARGUMENT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00741}00741 \textcolor{comment}{!         AND NONNEGATIVE ORDER BY D. E. AMOS, SAND85-\/1018, MAY 1985}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00742}00742 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00743}00743 \textcolor{comment}{!       A PORTABLE PACKAGE FOR BESSEL FUNCTIONS OF A COMPLEX ARGUMENT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00744}00744 \textcolor{comment}{!         AND NONNEGATIVE ORDER BY D. E. AMOS, ACM TRANS. MATH. SOFTWARE,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00745}00745 \textcolor{comment}{!         VOL. 12, NO. 3, SEPTEMBER 1986, PP 265-\/273.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00746}00746 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00747}00747 \textcolor{comment}{!***ROUTINES CALLED  CBINU,I1MACH,R1MACH}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00748}00748 \textcolor{comment}{!***END PROLOGUE  CBESJ}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00749}00749 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00750}00750 \textcolor{keywordtype}{COMPLEX (dp)}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{INTENT(IN)}   :: z}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00751}00751 real(dp), \textcolor{keywordtype}{INTENT(IN)}      :: fnu}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00752}00752 \textcolor{keywordtype}{INTEGER}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{INTENT(IN)}        :: kode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00753}00753 \textcolor{keywordtype}{INTEGER}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{INTENT(IN)}        :: n}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00754}00754 \textcolor{keywordtype}{COMPLEX (dp)}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{INTENT(OUT)}  :: cy(n)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00755}00755 \textcolor{keywordtype}{INTEGER}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{INTENT(OUT)}       :: nz}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00759}00759 real(dp)     :: aa, alim, arg, dig, elim, fnul, rl, r1, r1m5, r2,  \&}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00760}00760                  tol, yy, az, fn, bb, ascle, rtol, atol}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00761}00761 \textcolor{keywordtype}{INTEGER}       :: i, inu, inuh, ir, k1, k2, nl, k}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00762}00762 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00763}00763 real(dp), \textcolor{keywordtype}{PARAMETER}  :: hpi = 1.570796326794896619\_dp}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00764}00764 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00765}00765 \textcolor{comment}{!***FIRST EXECUTABLE STATEMENT  CBESJ}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00766}00766 ierr = 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00767}00767 nz = 0}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00770}00770 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (n < 1) ierr = 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00771}00771 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (ierr /= 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{RETURN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00772}00772 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00773}00773 \textcolor{comment}{!     SET PARAMETERS RELATED TO MACHINE CONSTANTS.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00774}00774 \textcolor{comment}{!     TOL IS THE APPROXIMATE UNIT ROUNDOFF LIMITED TO 1.0E-\/18.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00775}00775 \textcolor{comment}{!     ELIM IS THE APPROXIMATE EXPONENTIAL OVER-\/ AND UNDERFLOW LIMIT.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00776}00776 \textcolor{comment}{!     EXP(-\/ELIM) < EXP(-\/ALIM)=EXP(-\/ELIM)/TOL    AND}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00777}00777 \textcolor{comment}{!     EXP(ELIM) > EXP(ALIM)=EXP(ELIM)*TOL       ARE INTERVALS NEAR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00778}00778 \textcolor{comment}{!     UNDERFLOW AND OVERFLOW LIMITS WHERE SCALED ARITHMETIC IS DONE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00779}00779 \textcolor{comment}{!     RL IS THE LOWER BOUNDARY OF THE ASYMPTOTIC EXPANSION FOR LARGE Z.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00780}00780 \textcolor{comment}{!     DIG = NUMBER OF BASE 10 DIGITS IN TOL = 10**(-\/DIG).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00781}00781 \textcolor{comment}{!     FNUL IS THE LOWER BOUNDARY OF THE ASYMPTOTIC SERIES FOR LARGE FNU.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00782}00782 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00783}00783 tol = max(epsilon(0.0\_dp), 1.0d-\/18)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00784}00784 k1 = minexponent(0.0\_dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00785}00785 k2 = maxexponent(0.0\_dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00786}00786 r1m5 = log10( real( radix(0.0\_dp), kind=dp) )}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00787}00787 k = min(abs(k1),abs(k2))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00788}00788 elim = 2.303\_dp * (k*r1m5 -\/ 3.0\_dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00789}00789 k1 = digits(0.0\_dp) -\/ 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00790}00790 aa = r1m5 * k1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00791}00791 dig = min(aa, 18.0\_dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00792}00792 aa = aa * 2.303\_dp}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00793}00793 alim = elim + max(-\/aa, -\/41.45\_dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00794}00794 rl = 1.2\_dp * dig + 3.0\_dp}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00795}00795 fnul = 10.0\_dp + 6.0\_dp * (dig -\/ 3.0\_dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00796}00796 ci = cmplx(0.0\_dp, 1.0\_dp, kind=dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00797}00797 yy = aimag(z)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00798}00798 az = abs(z)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00799}00799 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00800}00800 \textcolor{comment}{!     TEST FOR RANGE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00801}00801 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00802}00802 aa = 0.5\_dp / tol}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00803}00803 bb = huge(0) * 0.5\_dp}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00804}00804 aa = min(aa,bb)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00805}00805 fn = fnu + (n-\/1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00806}00806 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (az <= aa) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00807}00807   \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (fn <= aa) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00808}00808     aa = sqrt(aa)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00809}00809     \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (az > aa) ierr = 3}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00810}00810     \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (fn > aa) ierr = 3}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00811}00811 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00812}00812 \textcolor{comment}{!     CALCULATE CSGN=EXP(FNU*HPI*I) TO MINIMIZE LOSSES OF SIGNIFICANCE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00813}00813 \textcolor{comment}{!     WHEN FNU IS LARGE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00814}00814 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00815}00815     inu = fnu}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00816}00816     inuh = inu / 2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00817}00817     ir = inu -\/ 2 * inuh}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00818}00818     arg = (fnu -\/ (inu-\/ir)) * hpi}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00819}00819     r1 = cos(arg)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00820}00820     r2 = sin(arg)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00821}00821     csgn = cmplx(r1, r2, kind=dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00822}00822     \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (mod(inuh,2) == 1) csgn = -\/csgn}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00823}00823 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00824}00824 \textcolor{comment}{!     ZN IS IN THE RIGHT HALF PLANE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00825}00825 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00826}00826     zn = -\/z * ci}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00827}00827     \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (yy < 0.0\_dp) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00828}00828       zn = -\/zn}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00829}00829       csgn = conjg(csgn)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00830}00830       ci = conjg(ci)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00831}00831 \textcolor{keywordflow}{    END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00832}00832     \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }cbinu(zn, fnu, kode, n, cy, nz, rl, fnul, tol, elim, alim)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00833}00833     \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (nz >= 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00834}00834       nl = n -\/ nz}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00835}00835       \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (nl == 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{RETURN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00836}00836       rtol = 1.0\_dp / tol}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00837}00837       ascle = tiny(0.0\_dp) * rtol * 1.0e+3}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00838}00838       \textcolor{keywordflow}{DO}  i = 1, nl}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00839}00839 \textcolor{comment}{!       CY(I)=CY(I)*CSGN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00840}00840         zn = cy(i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00841}00841         aa = real(zn, kind=dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00842}00842         bb = aimag(zn)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00843}00843         atol = 1.0\_dp}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00844}00844         \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (max(abs(aa),abs(bb)) <= ascle) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00845}00845           zn = zn * rtol}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00846}00846           atol = tol}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00847}00847 \textcolor{keywordflow}{        END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00848}00848         zn = zn * csgn}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00849}00849         cy(i) = zn * atol}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00850}00850         csgn = csgn * ci}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00851}00851 \textcolor{keywordflow}{      END DO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00852}00852       \textcolor{keywordflow}{RETURN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00853}00853 \textcolor{keywordflow}{    END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00854}00854     \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (nz /= -\/2) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00855}00855       nz = 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00856}00856       ierr = 2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00857}00857       \textcolor{keywordflow}{RETURN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00858}00858 \textcolor{keywordflow}{    END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00859}00859     nz = 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00860}00860     ierr = 5}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00861}00861     \textcolor{keywordflow}{RETURN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00862}00862 \textcolor{keywordflow}{  END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00863}00863 \textcolor{keywordflow}{END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00864}00864 nz = 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00865}00865 ierr = 4}
