\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00871}00871 \textcolor{keyword}{SUBROUTINE }cbesk(z, fnu, kode, n, cy, nz, ierr)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00872}00872 \textcolor{comment}{!***BEGIN PROLOGUE  CBESK}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00873}00873 \textcolor{comment}{!***DATE WRITTEN   830501   (YYMMDD)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00874}00874 \textcolor{comment}{!***REVISION DATE  890801, 930101   (YYMMDD)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00875}00875 \textcolor{comment}{!***CATEGORY NO.  B5K}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00876}00876 \textcolor{comment}{!***KEYWORDS  K-\/BESSEL FUNCTION,COMPLEX BESSEL FUNCTION,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00877}00877 \textcolor{comment}{!             MODIFIED BESSEL FUNCTION OF THE SECOND KIND,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00878}00878 \textcolor{comment}{!             BESSEL FUNCTION OF THE THIRD KIND}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00879}00879 \textcolor{comment}{!***AUTHOR  AMOS, DONALD E., SANDIA NATIONAL LABORATORIES}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00880}00880 \textcolor{comment}{!***PURPOSE  TO COMPUTE K-\/BESSEL FUNCTIONS OF COMPLEX ARGUMENT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00881}00881 \textcolor{comment}{!***DESCRIPTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00882}00882 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00883}00883 \textcolor{comment}{!   ON KODE=1, CBESK COMPUTES AN N MEMBER SEQUENCE OF COMPLEX BESSEL FUNCTIONS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00884}00884 \textcolor{comment}{!   CY(J)=K(FNU+J-\/1,Z) FOR REAL (dp), NONNEGATIVE ORDERS FNU+J-\/1, J=1,...,N}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00885}00885 \textcolor{comment}{!   AND COMPLEX Z.NE.CMPLX(0.0,0.0) IN THE CUT PLANE -\/PI < ARG(Z) <= PI.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00886}00886 \textcolor{comment}{!   ON KODE=2, CBESK RETURNS THE SCALED K FUNCTIONS,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00887}00887 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00888}00888 \textcolor{comment}{!   CY(J)=EXP(Z)*K(FNU+J-\/1,Z) , J=1,...,N,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00889}00889 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00890}00890 \textcolor{comment}{!   WHICH REMOVE THE EXPONENTIAL BEHAVIOR IN BOTH THE LEFT AND RIGHT HALF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00891}00891 \textcolor{comment}{!   PLANES FOR Z TO INFINITY.  DEFINITIONS AND NOTATION ARE FOUND IN THE NBS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00892}00892 \textcolor{comment}{!   HANDBOOK OF MATHEMATICAL FUNCTIONS (REF. 1).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00893}00893 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00894}00894 \textcolor{comment}{!   INPUT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00895}00895 \textcolor{comment}{!     Z      -\/ Z=CMPLX(X,Y),Z.NE.CMPLX(0.,0.),-\/PI < ARG(Z) <= PI}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00896}00896 \textcolor{comment}{!     FNU    -\/ ORDER OF INITIAL K FUNCTION, FNU >= 0.0\_dp}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00897}00897 \textcolor{comment}{!     N      -\/ NUMBER OF MEMBERS OF THE SEQUENCE, N >= 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00898}00898 \textcolor{comment}{!     KODE   -\/ A PARAMETER TO INDICATE THE SCALING OPTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00899}00899 \textcolor{comment}{!              KODE= 1  RETURNS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00900}00900 \textcolor{comment}{!                       CY(I)=K(FNU+I-\/1,Z), I=1,...,N}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00901}00901 \textcolor{comment}{!                  = 2  RETURNS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00902}00902 \textcolor{comment}{!                       CY(I)=K(FNU+I-\/1,Z)*EXP(Z), I=1,...,N}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00903}00903 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00904}00904 \textcolor{comment}{!   OUTPUT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00905}00905 \textcolor{comment}{!     CY     -\/ A COMPLEX VECTOR WHOSE FIRST N COMPONENTS CONTAIN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00906}00906 \textcolor{comment}{!              VALUES FOR THE SEQUENCE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00907}00907 \textcolor{comment}{!              CY(I)=K(FNU+I-\/1,Z), I=1,...,N OR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00908}00908 \textcolor{comment}{!              CY(I)=K(FNU+I-\/1,Z)*EXP(Z), I=1,...,N}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00909}00909 \textcolor{comment}{!              DEPENDING ON KODE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00910}00910 \textcolor{comment}{!     NZ     -\/ NUMBER OF COMPONENTS SET TO ZERO DUE TO UNDERFLOW.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00911}00911 \textcolor{comment}{!              NZ= 0   , NORMAL RETURN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00912}00912 \textcolor{comment}{!              NZ > 0 , FIRST NZ COMPONENTS OF CY SET TO ZERO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00913}00913 \textcolor{comment}{!                        DUE TO UNDERFLOW, CY(I)=CMPLX(0.0,0.0),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00914}00914 \textcolor{comment}{!                        I=1,...,N WHEN X >= 0.0.  WHEN X < 0.0, NZ STATES}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00915}00915 \textcolor{comment}{!                        ONLY THE NUMBER OF UNDERFLOWS IN THE SEQUENCE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00916}00916 \textcolor{comment}{!     IERR   -\/ ERROR FLAG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00917}00917 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=0, NORMAL RETURN -\/ COMPUTATION COMPLETED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00918}00918 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=1, INPUT ERROR   -\/ NO COMPUTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00919}00919 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=2, OVERFLOW      -\/ NO COMPUTATION, FNU+N-\/1 IS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00920}00920 \textcolor{comment}{!                      TOO LARGE OR ABS(Z) IS TOO SMALL OR BOTH}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00921}00921 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=3, ABS(Z) OR FNU+N-\/1 LARGE -\/ COMPUTATION DONE, BUT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00922}00922 \textcolor{comment}{!                      LOSSES OF SIGNIFICANCE BY ARGUMENT REDUCTION PRODUCE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00923}00923 \textcolor{comment}{!                      LESS THAN HALF OF MACHINE ACCURACY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00924}00924 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=4, ABS(Z) OR FNU+N-\/1 TOO LARGE -\/ NO COMPUTATION BECAUSE OF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00925}00925 \textcolor{comment}{!                      COMPLETE LOSSES OF SIGNIFICANCE BY ARGUMENT REDUCTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00926}00926 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=5, ERROR              -\/ NO COMPUTATION,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00927}00927 \textcolor{comment}{!                      ALGORITHM TERMINATION CONDITION NOT MET}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00928}00928 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00929}00929 \textcolor{comment}{!***LONG DESCRIPTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00930}00930 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00931}00931 \textcolor{comment}{!   EQUATIONS OF THE REFERENCE ARE IMPLEMENTED FOR SMALL ORDERS DNU AND}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00932}00932 \textcolor{comment}{!   DNU+1.0 IN THE RIGHT HALF PLANE X >= 0.0.  FORWARD RECURRENCE GENERATES}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00933}00933 \textcolor{comment}{!   HIGHER ORDERS.  K IS CONTINUED TO THE LEFT HALF PLANE BY THE RELATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00934}00934 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00935}00935 \textcolor{comment}{!   K(FNU,Z*EXP(MP)) = EXP(-\/MP*FNU)*K(FNU,Z)-\/MP*I(FNU,Z)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00936}00936 \textcolor{comment}{!   MP=MR*PI*I, MR=+1 OR -\/1, RE(Z) > 0, I**2=-\/1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00937}00937 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00938}00938 \textcolor{comment}{!   WHERE I(FNU,Z) IS THE I BESSEL FUNCTION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00939}00939 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00940}00940 \textcolor{comment}{!   FOR LARGE ORDERS, FNU > FNUL, THE K FUNCTION IS COMPUTED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00941}00941 \textcolor{comment}{!   BY MEANS OF ITS UNIFORM ASYMPTOTIC EXPANSIONS.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00942}00942 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00943}00943 \textcolor{comment}{!   FOR NEGATIVE ORDERS, THE FORMULA}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00944}00944 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00945}00945 \textcolor{comment}{!                 K(-\/FNU,Z) = K(FNU,Z)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00946}00946 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00947}00947 \textcolor{comment}{!   CAN BE USED.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00948}00948 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00949}00949 \textcolor{comment}{!   CBESK ASSUMES THAT A SIGNIFICANT DIGIT SINH(X) FUNCTION IS AVAILABLE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00950}00950 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00951}00951 \textcolor{comment}{!   IN MOST COMPLEX VARIABLE COMPUTATION, ONE MUST EVALUATE ELEMENTARY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00952}00952 \textcolor{comment}{!   FUNCTIONS.  WHEN THE MAGNITUDE OF Z OR FNU+N-\/1 IS LARGE, LOSSES OF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00953}00953 \textcolor{comment}{!   SIGNIFICANCE BY ARGUMENT REDUCTION OCCUR.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00954}00954 \textcolor{comment}{!   CONSEQUENTLY, IF EITHER ONE EXCEEDS U1=SQRT(0.5/UR), THEN LOSSES EXCEEDING}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00955}00955 \textcolor{comment}{!   HALF PRECISION ARE LIKELY AND AN ERROR FLAG IERR=3 IS TRIGGERED WHERE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00956}00956 \textcolor{comment}{!   UR = EPSILON(0.0\_dp) = UNIT ROUNDOFF.  ALSO IF EITHER IS LARGER THAN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00957}00957 \textcolor{comment}{!   U2 = 0.5/UR, THEN ALL SIGNIFICANCE IS LOST AND IERR=4.  IN ORDER TO USE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00958}00958 \textcolor{comment}{!   THE INT FUNCTION, ARGUMENTS MUST BE FURTHER RESTRICTED NOT TO EXCEED THE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00959}00959 \textcolor{comment}{!   LARGEST MACHINE INTEGER, U3=HUGE(0).  THUS, THE MAGNITUDE OF Z AND FNU+N-\/1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00960}00960 \textcolor{comment}{!   IS RESTRICTED BY MIN(U2,U3).  ON 32 BIT MACHINES, U1,U2, AND U3 ARE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00961}00961 \textcolor{comment}{!   APPROXIMATELY 2.0E+3, 4.2E+6, 2.1E+9 IN SINGLE PRECISION ARITHMETIC AND}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00962}00962 \textcolor{comment}{!   1.3E+8, 1.8D+16, 2.1E+9 IN DOUBLE PRECISION ARITHMETIC RESPECTIVELY.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00963}00963 \textcolor{comment}{!   THIS MAKES U2 AND U3 LIMITING IN THEIR RESPECTIVE ARITHMETICS.  THIS MEANS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00964}00964 \textcolor{comment}{!   THAT ONE CAN EXPECT TO RETAIN, IN THE WORST CASES ON 32 BIT MACHINES, NO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00965}00965 \textcolor{comment}{!   DIGITS IN SINGLE AND ONLY 7 DIGITS IN DOUBLE PRECISION ARITHMETIC.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00966}00966 \textcolor{comment}{!   SIMILAR CONSIDERATIONS HOLD FOR OTHER MACHINES.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00967}00967 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00968}00968 \textcolor{comment}{!   THE APPROXIMATE RELATIVE ERROR IN THE MAGNITUDE OF A COMPLEX BESSEL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00969}00969 \textcolor{comment}{!   FUNCTION CAN BE EXPRESSED BY P*10**S WHERE P = MAX(UNIT ROUNDOFF,1.0E-\/18)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00970}00970 \textcolor{comment}{!   IS THE NOMINAL PRECISION AND 10**S REPRESENTS THE INCREASE IN ERROR DUE TO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00971}00971 \textcolor{comment}{!   ARGUMENT REDUCTION IN THE ELEMENTARY FUNCTIONS.  HERE, S =}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00972}00972 \textcolor{comment}{!   MAX(1,ABS(LOG10(ABS(Z))), ABS(LOG10(FNU))) APPROXIMATELY (I.E. S =}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00973}00973 \textcolor{comment}{!   MAX(1,ABS(EXPONENT OF ABS(Z),ABS(EXPONENT OF FNU)) ).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00974}00974 \textcolor{comment}{!   HOWEVER, THE PHASE ANGLE MAY HAVE ONLY ABSOLUTE ACCURACY.  THIS IS MOST}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00975}00975 \textcolor{comment}{!   LIKELY TO OCCUR WHEN ONE COMPONENT (IN ABSOLUTE VALUE) IS LARGER THAN THE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00976}00976 \textcolor{comment}{!   OTHER BY SEVERAL ORDERS OF MAGNITUDE.  IF ONE COMPONENT IS 10**K LARGER}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00977}00977 \textcolor{comment}{!   THAN THE OTHER, THEN ONE CAN EXPECT ONLY MAX(ABS(LOG10(P))-\/K, 0)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00978}00978 \textcolor{comment}{!   SIGNIFICANT DIGITS; OR, STATED ANOTHER WAY, WHEN K EXCEEDS THE EXPONENT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00979}00979 \textcolor{comment}{!   OF P, NO SIGNIFICANT DIGITS REMAIN IN THE SMALLER COMPONENT.  HOWEVER, THE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00980}00980 \textcolor{comment}{!   PHASE ANGLE RETAINS ABSOLUTE ACCURACY BECAUSE, IN COMPLEX ARITHMETIC WITH}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00981}00981 \textcolor{comment}{!   PRECISION P, THE SMALLER COMPONENT WILL NOT (AS A RULE) DECREASE BELOW P}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00982}00982 \textcolor{comment}{!   TIMES THE MAGNITUDE OF THE LARGER COMPONENT.  IN THESE EXTREME CASES,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00983}00983 \textcolor{comment}{!   THE PRINCIPAL PHASE ANGLE IS ON THE ORDER OF +P, -\/P, PI/2-\/P, OR -\/PI/2+P.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00984}00984 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00985}00985 \textcolor{comment}{!***REFERENCES  HANDBOOK OF MATHEMATICAL FUNCTIONS BY M. ABRAMOWITZ AND}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00986}00986 \textcolor{comment}{!           I. A. STEGUN, NBS AMS SERIES 55, U.S. DEPT. OF COMMERCE, 1955.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00987}00987 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00988}00988 \textcolor{comment}{!         COMPUTATION OF BESSEL FUNCTIONS OF COMPLEX ARGUMENT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00989}00989 \textcolor{comment}{!           BY D. E. AMOS, SAND83-\/0083, MAY 1983.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00990}00990 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00991}00991 \textcolor{comment}{!         COMPUTATION OF BESSEL FUNCTIONS OF COMPLEX ARGUMENT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00992}00992 \textcolor{comment}{!           AND LARGE ORDER BY D. E. AMOS, SAND83-\/0643, MAY 1983.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00995}00995 \textcolor{comment}{!           AND NONNEGATIVE ORDER BY D. E. AMOS, SAND85-\/1018, MAY 1985}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l00998}00998 \textcolor{comment}{!           AND NONNEGATIVE ORDER BY D. E. AMOS, ACM TRANS. MATH. SOFTWARE,}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01001}01001 \textcolor{comment}{!***ROUTINES CALLED  CACON,CBKNU,CBUNK,CUOIK,I1MACH,R1MACH}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01002}01002 \textcolor{comment}{!***END PROLOGUE  CBESK}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01003}01003 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01004}01004 \textcolor{keywordtype}{COMPLEX (dp)}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{INTENT(IN)}   :: z}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01005}01005 real(dp), \textcolor{keywordtype}{INTENT(IN)}      :: fnu}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01006}01006 \textcolor{keywordtype}{INTEGER}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{INTENT(IN)}        :: kode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01007}01007 \textcolor{keywordtype}{INTEGER}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{INTENT(IN)}        :: n}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01008}01008 \textcolor{keywordtype}{COMPLEX (dp)}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{INTENT(OUT)}  :: cy(n)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01009}01009 \textcolor{keywordtype}{INTEGER}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{INTENT(OUT)}       :: nz}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01010}01010 \textcolor{keywordtype}{INTEGER}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{INTENT(OUT)}       :: ierr}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01011}01011 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01012}01012 real(dp)  :: aa, alim, aln, arg, az, dig, elim, fn, fnul, rl, r1m5,  \&}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01013}01013               tol, ufl, xx, yy, bb}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01014}01014 \textcolor{keywordtype}{INTEGER}    :: k, k1, k2, mr, nn, nuf, nw}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01015}01015 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01016}01016 \textcolor{comment}{!***FIRST EXECUTABLE STATEMENT  CBESK}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01017}01017 ierr = 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01018}01018 nz = 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01019}01019 xx = real(z, kind=dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01020}01020 yy = aimag(z)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01021}01021 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (yy == 0.0\_dp .AND. xx == 0.0\_dp) ierr = 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01022}01022 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (fnu < 0.0\_dp) ierr = 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01023}01023 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (kode < 1 .OR. kode > 2) ierr = 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01024}01024 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (n < 1) ierr = 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01025}01025 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (ierr /= 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{RETURN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01026}01026 nn = n}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01027}01027 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01028}01028 \textcolor{comment}{!     SET PARAMETERS RELATED TO MACHINE CONSTANTS.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01029}01029 \textcolor{comment}{!     TOL IS THE APPROXIMATE UNIT ROUNDOFF LIMITED TO 1.0E-\/18.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01030}01030 \textcolor{comment}{!     ELIM IS THE APPROXIMATE EXPONENTIAL OVER-\/ AND UNDERFLOW LIMIT.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01031}01031 \textcolor{comment}{!     EXP(-\/ELIM) < EXP(-\/ALIM)=EXP(-\/ELIM)/TOL    AND}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01032}01032 \textcolor{comment}{!     EXP(ELIM) > EXP(ALIM)=EXP(ELIM)*TOL       ARE INTERVALS NEAR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01033}01033 \textcolor{comment}{!     UNDERFLOW AND OVERFLOW LIMITS WHERE SCALED ARITHMETIC IS DONE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01034}01034 \textcolor{comment}{!     RL IS THE LOWER BOUNDARY OF THE ASYMPTOTIC EXPANSION FOR LARGE Z.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01035}01035 \textcolor{comment}{!     DIG = NUMBER OF BASE 10 DIGITS IN TOL = 10**(-\/DIG).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01036}01036 \textcolor{comment}{!     FNUL IS THE LOWER BOUNDARY OF THE ASYMPTOTIC SERIES FOR LARGE FNU}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01037}01037 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01038}01038 tol = max(epsilon(0.0\_dp), 1.0d-\/18)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01039}01039 k1 = minexponent(0.0\_dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01040}01040 k2 = maxexponent(0.0\_dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01041}01041 r1m5 = log10( real( radix(0.0\_dp), kind=dp) )}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01042}01042 k = min(abs(k1),abs(k2))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01043}01043 elim = 2.303\_dp * (k*r1m5 -\/ 3.0\_dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01044}01044 k1 = digits(0.0\_dp) -\/ 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01045}01045 aa = r1m5 * k1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01046}01046 dig = min(aa, 18.0\_dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01047}01047 aa = aa * 2.303\_dp}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01048}01048 alim = elim + max(-\/aa, -\/41.45\_dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01049}01049 fnul = 10.0\_dp + 6.0\_dp * (dig -\/ 3.0\_dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01050}01050 rl = 1.2\_dp * dig + 3.0\_dp}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01051}01051 az = abs(z)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01052}01052 fn = fnu + (nn-\/1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01053}01053 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01054}01054 \textcolor{comment}{!     TEST FOR RANGE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01055}01055 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01056}01056 aa = 0.5\_dp / tol}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01057}01057 bb = huge(0) * 0.5\_dp}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01058}01058 aa = min(aa,bb)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01059}01059 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (az <= aa) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01060}01060   \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (fn <= aa) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01061}01061     aa = sqrt(aa)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01062}01062     \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (az > aa) ierr = 3}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01063}01063     \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (fn > aa) ierr = 3}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01064}01064 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01065}01065 \textcolor{comment}{!     OVERFLOW TEST ON THE LAST MEMBER OF THE SEQUENCE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01066}01066 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01067}01067 \textcolor{comment}{!     UFL = EXP(-\/ELIM)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01068}01068     ufl = tiny(0.0\_dp) * 1.0e+3}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01069}01069     \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (az >= ufl) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01070}01070       \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (fnu <= fnul) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01081}01081             nn = nn -\/ nuf}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01148}01148 \textcolor{comment}{!***BEGIN PROLOGUE  CBESY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01149}01149 \textcolor{comment}{!***DATE WRITTEN   830501   (YYMMDD)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01150}01150 \textcolor{comment}{!***REVISION DATE  890801, 930101  (YYMMDD)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01151}01151 \textcolor{comment}{!***CATEGORY NO.  B5K}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01152}01152 \textcolor{comment}{!***KEYWORDS  Y-\/BESSEL FUNCTION,BESSEL FUNCTION OF COMPLEX ARGUMENT,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01153}01153 \textcolor{comment}{!             BESSEL FUNCTION OF SECOND KIND}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01154}01154 \textcolor{comment}{!***AUTHOR  AMOS, DONALD E., SANDIA NATIONAL LABORATORIES}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01155}01155 \textcolor{comment}{!***PURPOSE  TO COMPUTE THE Y-\/BESSEL FUNCTION OF A COMPLEX ARGUMENT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01156}01156 \textcolor{comment}{!***DESCRIPTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01157}01157 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01158}01158 \textcolor{comment}{!   ON KODE=1, CBESY COMPUTES AN N MEMBER SEQUENCE OF COMPLEX}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01159}01159 \textcolor{comment}{!   BESSEL FUNCTIONS CY(I)=Y(FNU+I-\/1,Z) FOR REAL (dp), NONNEGATIVE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01160}01160 \textcolor{comment}{!   ORDERS FNU+I-\/1, I=1,...,N AND COMPLEX Z IN THE CUT PLANE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01161}01161 \textcolor{comment}{!   -\/PI < ARG(Z) <= PI.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01162}01162 \textcolor{comment}{!   ON KODE=2, CBESY RETURNS THE SCALED FUNCTIONS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01163}01163 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01164}01164 \textcolor{comment}{!   CY(I)=EXP(-\/ABS(Y))*Y(FNU+I-\/1,Z)   I = 1,...,N , Y=AIMAG(Z)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01165}01165 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01166}01166 \textcolor{comment}{!   WHICH REMOVE THE EXPONENTIAL GROWTH IN BOTH THE UPPER AND}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01167}01167 \textcolor{comment}{!   LOWER HALF PLANES FOR Z TO INFINITY. DEFINITIONS AND NOTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01168}01168 \textcolor{comment}{!   ARE FOUND IN THE NBS HANDBOOK OF MATHEMATICAL FUNCTIONS (REF. 1).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01169}01169 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01170}01170 \textcolor{comment}{!   INPUT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01171}01171 \textcolor{comment}{!     Z      -\/ Z=CMPLX(X,Y), Z.NE.CMPLX(0.,0.),-\/PI < ARG(Z) <= PI}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01172}01172 \textcolor{comment}{!     FNU    -\/ ORDER OF INITIAL Y FUNCTION, FNU >= 0.0\_dp}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01173}01173 \textcolor{comment}{!     KODE   -\/ A PARAMETER TO INDICATE THE SCALING OPTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01174}01174 \textcolor{comment}{!              KODE= 1  RETURNS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01175}01175 \textcolor{comment}{!                       CY(I)=Y(FNU+I-\/1,Z), I=1,...,N}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01176}01176 \textcolor{comment}{!                  = 2  RETURNS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01177}01177 \textcolor{comment}{!                       CY(I)=Y(FNU+I-\/1,Z)*EXP(-\/ABS(Y)), I=1,...,N}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01178}01178 \textcolor{comment}{!                       WHERE Y=AIMAG(Z)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01179}01179 \textcolor{comment}{!     N      -\/ NUMBER OF MEMBERS OF THE SEQUENCE, N >= 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01180}01180 \textcolor{comment}{!     CWRK   -\/ A COMPLEX WORK VECTOR OF DIMENSION AT LEAST N}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01181}01181 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01182}01182 \textcolor{comment}{!   OUTPUT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01183}01183 \textcolor{comment}{!     CY     -\/ A COMPLEX VECTOR WHOSE FIRST N COMPONENTS CONTAIN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01184}01184 \textcolor{comment}{!              VALUES FOR THE SEQUENCE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01185}01185 \textcolor{comment}{!              CY(I)=Y(FNU+I-\/1,Z)  OR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01186}01186 \textcolor{comment}{!              CY(I)=Y(FNU+I-\/1,Z)*EXP(-\/ABS(Y))  I=1,...,N}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01187}01187 \textcolor{comment}{!              DEPENDING ON KODE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01188}01188 \textcolor{comment}{!     NZ     -\/ NZ=0 , A NORMAL RETURN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01189}01189 \textcolor{comment}{!              NZ > 0 , NZ COMPONENTS OF CY SET TO ZERO DUE TO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01190}01190 \textcolor{comment}{!              UNDERFLOW (GENERALLY ON KODE=2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01191}01191 \textcolor{comment}{!     IERR   -\/ ERROR FLAG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01192}01192 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=0, NORMAL RETURN -\/ COMPUTATION COMPLETED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01193}01193 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=1, INPUT ERROR   -\/ NO COMPUTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01194}01194 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=2, OVERFLOW      -\/ NO COMPUTATION, FNU+N-\/1 IS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01195}01195 \textcolor{comment}{!                      TOO LARGE OR ABS(Z) IS TOO SMALL OR BOTH}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01196}01196 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=3, ABS(Z) OR FNU+N-\/1 LARGE -\/ COMPUTATION DONE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01197}01197 \textcolor{comment}{!                      BUT LOSSES OF SIGNIFICANCE BY ARGUMENT REDUCTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01198}01198 \textcolor{comment}{!                      PRODUCE LESS THAN HALF OF MACHINE ACCURACY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01199}01199 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=4, ABS(Z) OR FNU+N-\/1 TOO LARGE -\/ NO COMPUTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01200}01200 \textcolor{comment}{!                      BECAUSE OF COMPLETE LOSSES OF SIGNIFICANCE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01201}01201 \textcolor{comment}{!                      BY ARGUMENT REDUCTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01202}01202 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=5, ERROR              -\/ NO COMPUTATION,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01203}01203 \textcolor{comment}{!                      ALGORITHM TERMINATION CONDITION NOT MET}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01204}01204 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01205}01205 \textcolor{comment}{!***LONG DESCRIPTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01206}01206 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01207}01207 \textcolor{comment}{!   THE COMPUTATION IS CARRIED OUT IN TERMS OF THE I(FNU,Z) AND}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01208}01208 \textcolor{comment}{!   K(FNU,Z) BESSEL FUNCTIONS IN THE RIGHT HALF PLANE BY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01209}01209 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01210}01210 \textcolor{comment}{!       Y(FNU,Z) = I*CC*I(FNU,ARG) -\/ (2/PI)*CONJG(CC)*K(FNU,ARG)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01211}01211 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01212}01212 \textcolor{comment}{!       Y(FNU,Z) = CONJG(Y(FNU,CONJG(Z)))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01213}01213 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01214}01214 \textcolor{comment}{!   FOR AIMAG(Z) >= 0 AND AIMAG(Z) < 0 RESPECTIVELY, WHERE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01215}01215 \textcolor{comment}{!   CC=EXP(I*PI*FNU/2), ARG=Z*EXP(-\/I*PI/2) AND I**2=-\/1.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01216}01216 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01217}01217 \textcolor{comment}{!   FOR NEGATIVE ORDERS,THE FORMULA}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01218}01218 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01219}01219 \textcolor{comment}{!       Y(-\/FNU,Z) = Y(FNU,Z)*COS(PI*FNU) + J(FNU,Z)*SIN(PI*FNU)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01220}01220 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01221}01221 \textcolor{comment}{!   CAN BE USED.  HOWEVER,FOR LARGE ORDERS CLOSE TO HALF ODD INTEGERS THE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01222}01222 \textcolor{comment}{!   FUNCTION CHANGES RADICALLY.  WHEN FNU IS A LARGE POSITIVE HALF ODD INTEGER,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01223}01223 \textcolor{comment}{!   THE MAGNITUDE OF Y(-\/FNU,Z) = J(FNU,Z)*SIN(PI*FNU) IS A LARGE NEGATIVE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01224}01224 \textcolor{comment}{!   POWER OF TEN.  BUT WHEN FNU IS NOT A HALF ODD INTEGER, Y(FNU,Z) DOMINATES}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01225}01225 \textcolor{comment}{!   IN MAGNITUDE WITH A LARGE POSITIVE POWER OF TEN AND THE MOST THAT THE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01226}01226 \textcolor{comment}{!   SECOND TERM CAN BE REDUCED IS BY UNIT ROUNDOFF FROM THE COEFFICIENT.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01227}01227 \textcolor{comment}{!   THUS, WIDE CHANGES CAN OCCUR WITHIN UNIT ROUNDOFF OF A LARGE HALF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01228}01228 \textcolor{comment}{!   ODD INTEGER.  HERE, LARGE MEANS FNU > ABS(Z).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01229}01229 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01230}01230 \textcolor{comment}{!   IN MOST COMPLEX VARIABLE COMPUTATION, ONE MUST EVALUATE ELEMENTARY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01231}01231 \textcolor{comment}{!   FUNCTIONS.  WHEN THE MAGNITUDE OF Z OR FNU+N-\/1 IS LARGE, LOSSES OF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01232}01232 \textcolor{comment}{!   SIGNIFICANCE BY ARGUMENT REDUCTION OCCUR.  CONSEQUENTLY, IF EITHER ONE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01233}01233 \textcolor{comment}{!   EXCEEDS U1=SQRT(0.5/UR), THEN LOSSES EXCEEDING HALF PRECISION ARE LIKELY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01234}01234 \textcolor{comment}{!   AND AN ERROR FLAG IERR=3 IS TRIGGERED WHERE UR = EPSILON(0.0\_dp) = UNIT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01235}01235 \textcolor{comment}{!   ROUNDOFF.  ALSO IF EITHER IS LARGER THAN U2=0.5/UR, THEN ALL SIGNIFICANCE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01236}01236 \textcolor{comment}{!   IS LOST AND IERR=4.  IN ORDER TO USE THE INT FUNCTION, ARGUMENTS MUST BE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01237}01237 \textcolor{comment}{!   FURTHER RESTRICTED NOT TO EXCEED THE LARGEST MACHINE INTEGER, U3 = HUGE(0).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01238}01238 \textcolor{comment}{!   THUS, THE MAGNITUDE OF Z AND FNU+N-\/1 IS RESTRICTED BY MIN(U2,U3).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01239}01239 \textcolor{comment}{!   ON 32 BIT MACHINES, U1,U2, AND U3 ARE APPROXIMATELY 2.0E+3, 4.2E+6, 2.1E+9}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01240}01240 \textcolor{comment}{!   IN SINGLE PRECISION ARITHMETIC AND 1.3E+8, 1.8D+16, 2.1E+9 IN DOUBLE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01241}01241 \textcolor{comment}{!   PRECISION ARITHMETIC RESPECTIVELY. THIS MAKES U2 AND U3 LIMITING IN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01242}01242 \textcolor{comment}{!   THEIR RESPECTIVE ARITHMETICS.  THIS MEANS THAT ONE CAN EXPECT TO RETAIN,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01243}01243 \textcolor{comment}{!   IN THE WORST CASES ON 32 BIT MACHINES, NO DIGITS IN SINGLE AND ONLY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01244}01244 \textcolor{comment}{!   7 DIGITS IN DOUBLE PRECISION ARITHMETIC.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01245}01245 \textcolor{comment}{!   SIMILAR CONSIDERATIONS HOLD FOR OTHER MACHINES.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01246}01246 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01247}01247 \textcolor{comment}{!   THE APPROXIMATE RELATIVE ERROR IN THE MAGNITUDE OF A COMPLEX BESSEL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01248}01248 \textcolor{comment}{!   FUNCTION CAN BE EXPRESSED BY P*10**S WHERE P = MAX(UNIT ROUNDOFF,1.0E-\/18)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01249}01249 \textcolor{comment}{!   IS THE NOMINAL PRECISION AND 10**S REPRESENTS THE INCREASE IN ERROR DUE TO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01250}01250 \textcolor{comment}{!   ARGUMENT REDUCTION IN THE ELEMENTARY FUNCTIONS.  HERE, S =}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01251}01251 \textcolor{comment}{!   MAX(1,ABS(LOG10(ABS(Z))), ABS(LOG10(FNU))) APPROXIMATELY (I.E. S =}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01252}01252 \textcolor{comment}{!   MAX(1,ABS(EXPONENT OF ABS(Z),ABS(EXPONENT OF FNU)) ).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01253}01253 \textcolor{comment}{!   HOWEVER, THE PHASE ANGLE MAY HAVE ONLY ABSOLUTE ACCURACY.  THIS IS MOST}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01254}01254 \textcolor{comment}{!   LIKELY TO OCCUR WHEN ONE COMPONENT (IN ABSOLUTE VALUE) IS LARGER THAN THE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01255}01255 \textcolor{comment}{!   OTHER BY SEVERAL ORDERS OF MAGNITUDE.  IF ONE COMPONENT IS 10**K LARGER}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01256}01256 \textcolor{comment}{!   THAN THE OTHER, THEN ONE CAN EXPECT ONLY MAX(ABS(LOG10(P))-\/K, 0)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01257}01257 \textcolor{comment}{!   SIGNIFICANT DIGITS; OR, STATED ANOTHER WAY, WHEN K EXCEEDS THE EXPONENT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01258}01258 \textcolor{comment}{!   OF P, NO SIGNIFICANT DIGITS REMAIN IN THE SMALLER COMPONENT.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01259}01259 \textcolor{comment}{!   HOWEVER, THE PHASE ANGLE RETAINS ABSOLUTE ACCURACY BECAUSE, IN COMPLEX}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01260}01260 \textcolor{comment}{!   ARITHMETIC WITH PRECISION P, THE SMALLER COMPONENT WILL NOT (AS A RULE)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01261}01261 \textcolor{comment}{!   DECREASE BELOW P TIMES THE MAGNITUDE OF THE LARGER COMPONENT.  IN THESE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01262}01262 \textcolor{comment}{!   EXTREME CASES, THE PRINCIPAL PHASE ANGLE IS ON THE ORDER OF +P, -\/P,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01263}01263 \textcolor{comment}{!   PI/2-\/P, OR -\/PI/2+P.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01264}01264 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01265}01265 \textcolor{comment}{!***REFERENCES  HANDBOOK OF MATHEMATICAL FUNCTIONS BY M. ABRAMOWITZ AND}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01266}01266 \textcolor{comment}{!        I. A. STEGUN, NBS AMS SERIES 55, U.S. DEPT. OF COMMERCE, 1955.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01267}01267 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01268}01268 \textcolor{comment}{!      COMPUTATION OF BESSEL FUNCTIONS OF COMPLEX ARGUMENT}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01270}01270 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01297}01297                                         (-\/1.0\_dp, 0.0\_dp), (0.0\_dp, -\/1.0\_dp) /)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01298}01298 real(dp), \textcolor{keywordtype}{PARAMETER}     :: hpi = 1.57079632679489662\_dp}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01299}01299 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01300}01300 \textcolor{comment}{!***FIRST EXECUTABLE STATEMENT  CBESY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01301}01301 xx = real(z, kind=dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01302}01302 yy = aimag(z)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01303}01303 ierr = 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01304}01304 nz = 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01305}01305 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (xx == 0.0\_dp .AND. yy == 0.0\_dp) ierr = 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01306}01306 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (fnu < 0.0\_dp) ierr = 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01307}01307 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (kode < 1 .OR. kode > 2) ierr = 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01308}01308 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (n < 1) ierr = 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01309}01309 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (ierr /= 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{RETURN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01310}01310 ci = cmplx(0.0\_dp, 1.0\_dp, kind=dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01311}01311 zz = z}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01312}01312 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (yy < 0.0\_dp) zz = conjg(z)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01313}01313 zn = -\/ci * zz}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01314}01314 \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }cbesi(zn, fnu, kode, n, cy, nz1, ierr)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01315}01315 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (ierr == 0 .OR. ierr == 3) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01316}01316   \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }cbesk(zn, fnu, kode, n, cwrk, nz2, ierr)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01317}01317   \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (ierr == 0 .OR. ierr == 3) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01318}01318     nz = min(nz1, nz2)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01319}01319     ifnu = fnu}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01320}01320     ffnu = fnu -\/ ifnu}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01321}01321     arg = hpi * ffnu}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01322}01322     csgn = cmplx(cos(arg), sin(arg), kind=dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01323}01323     i4 = mod(ifnu, 4) + 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01324}01324     csgn = csgn * cip(i4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01325}01325     rhpi = 1.0\_dp / hpi}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01326}01326     cspn = conjg(csgn) * rhpi}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01327}01327     csgn = csgn * ci}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01328}01328     \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (kode /= 2) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01329}01329       \textcolor{keywordflow}{DO}  i = 1, n}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01330}01330         cy(i) = csgn * cy(i) -\/ cspn * cwrk(i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01331}01331         csgn = ci * csgn}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01332}01332         cspn = -\/ci * cspn}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01333}01333 \textcolor{keywordflow}{      END DO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01334}01334       \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (yy < 0.0\_dp) cy(1:n) = conjg(cy(1:n))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01335}01335       \textcolor{keywordflow}{RETURN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01336}01336 \textcolor{keywordflow}{    END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01337}01337 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01338}01338     r1 = cos(xx)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01339}01339     r2 = sin(xx)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01340}01340     ex = cmplx(r1, r2, kind=dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01341}01341     tol = max(epsilon(0.0\_dp), 1.0d-\/18)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01342}01342     k1 = minexponent(0.0\_dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01343}01343     k2 = maxexponent(0.0\_dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01344}01344     k = min(abs(k1),abs(k2))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01345}01345     r1m5 = log10( real( radix(0.0\_dp), kind=dp) )}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01346}01346 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01347}01347 \textcolor{comment}{!     ELIM IS THE APPROXIMATE EXPONENTIAL UNDER-\/ AND OVERFLOW LIMIT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01348}01348 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01349}01349     elim = 2.303\_dp * (k*r1m5 -\/ 3.0\_dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01350}01350     ey = 0.0\_dp}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01351}01351     tay = abs(yy+yy)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01352}01352     \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (tay < elim) ey = exp(-\/tay)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01353}01353     cspn = ex * ey * cspn}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01354}01354     nz = 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01355}01355     rtol = 1.0\_dp / tol}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01356}01356     ascle = tiny(0.0\_dp) * rtol * 1.0e+3}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01357}01357     \textcolor{keywordflow}{DO}  i = 1, n}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01358}01358 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01359}01359 \textcolor{comment}{!       CY(I) = CSGN*CY(I)-\/CSPN*CWRK(I): PRODUCTS ARE COMPUTED IN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01360}01360 \textcolor{comment}{!       SCALED MODE IF CY(I) OR CWRK(I) ARE CLOSE TO UNDERFLOW TO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01361}01361 \textcolor{comment}{!       PREVENT UNDERFLOW IN AN INTERMEDIATE COMPUTATION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01362}01362 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01363}01363       zv = cwrk(i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01364}01364       aa = real(zv, kind=dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01365}01365       bb = aimag(zv)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01366}01366       atol = 1.0\_dp}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01367}01367       \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (max(abs(aa),abs(bb)) <= ascle) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01368}01368         zv = zv * rtol}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01369}01369         atol = tol}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01370}01370 \textcolor{keywordflow}{      END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01371}01371       zv = zv * cspn}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01372}01372       zv = zv * atol}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01373}01373       zu = cy(i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01374}01374       aa = real(zu, kind=dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01375}01375       bb = aimag(zu)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01376}01376       atol = 1.0\_dp}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01377}01377       \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (max(abs(aa),abs(bb)) <= ascle) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01378}01378         zu = zu * rtol}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01379}01379         atol = tol}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01380}01380 \textcolor{keywordflow}{      END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01381}01381       zu = zu * csgn}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01382}01382       zu = zu * atol}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01383}01383       cy(i) = zu -\/ zv}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01384}01384       \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (yy < 0.0\_dp) cy(i) = conjg(cy(i))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01385}01385       \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (cy(i) == cmplx(0.0\_dp, 0.0\_dp, kind=dp) .AND. ey == 0.0\_dp) nz = nz + 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01386}01386       csgn = ci * csgn}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01387}01387       cspn = -\/ci * cspn}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01388}01388 \textcolor{keywordflow}{    END DO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01389}01389     \textcolor{keywordflow}{RETURN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01390}01390 \textcolor{keywordflow}{  END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01391}01391 \textcolor{keywordflow}{END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01392}01392 nz = 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01393}01393 \textcolor{keywordflow}{RETURN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01394}01394 \textcolor{keyword}{END SUBROUTINE }cbesy}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01395}01395 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01396}01396 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01397}01397 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01398}01398 \textcolor{keyword}{SUBROUTINE }cairy(z, id, kode, ai, nz, ierr)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01399}01399 \textcolor{comment}{!***BEGIN PROLOGUE  CAIRY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01400}01400 \textcolor{comment}{!***DATE WRITTEN   830501   (YYMMDD)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01401}01401 \textcolor{comment}{!***REVISION DATE  890801, 930101   (YYMMDD)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01402}01402 \textcolor{comment}{!***CATEGORY NO.  B5K}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01403}01403 \textcolor{comment}{!***KEYWORDS  AIRY FUNCTION,BESSEL FUNCTIONS OF ORDER ONE THIRD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01404}01404 \textcolor{comment}{!***AUTHOR  AMOS, DONALD E., SANDIA NATIONAL LABORATORIES}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01405}01405 \textcolor{comment}{!***PURPOSE  TO COMPUTE AIRY FUNCTIONS AI(Z) AND DAI(Z) FOR COMPLEX Z}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01406}01406 \textcolor{comment}{!***DESCRIPTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01407}01407 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01408}01408 \textcolor{comment}{!   ON KODE=1, CAIRY COMPUTES THE COMPLEX AIRY FUNCTION AI(Z) OR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01409}01409 \textcolor{comment}{!   ITS DERIVATIVE DAI(Z)/DZ ON ID=0 OR ID=1 RESPECTIVELY.  ON}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01410}01410 \textcolor{comment}{!   KODE=2, A SCALING OPTION EXP(ZTA)*AI(Z) OR EXP(ZTA)*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01411}01411 \textcolor{comment}{!   DAI(Z)/DZ IS PROVIDED TO REMOVE THE EXPONENTIAL DECAY IN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01412}01412 \textcolor{comment}{!   -\/PI/3 < ARG(Z) < PI/3 AND THE EXPONENTIAL GROWTH IN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01413}01413 \textcolor{comment}{!   PI/3 < ABS(ARG(Z)) < PI WHERE ZTA=(2/3)*Z*SQRT(Z)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01414}01414 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01415}01415 \textcolor{comment}{!   WHILE THE AIRY FUNCTIONS AI(Z) AND DAI(Z)/DZ ARE ANALYTIC IN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01416}01416 \textcolor{comment}{!   THE WHOLE Z PLANE, THE CORRESPONDING SCALED FUNCTIONS DEFINED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01417}01417 \textcolor{comment}{!   FOR KODE=2 HAVE A CUT ALONG THE NEGATIVE REAL AXIS.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01418}01418 \textcolor{comment}{!   DEFINITIONS AND NOTATION ARE FOUND IN THE NBS HANDBOOK OF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01419}01419 \textcolor{comment}{!   MATHEMATICAL FUNCTIONS (REF. 1).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01420}01420 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01421}01421 \textcolor{comment}{!   INPUT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01422}01422 \textcolor{comment}{!     Z      -\/ Z=CMPLX(X,Y)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01423}01423 \textcolor{comment}{!     ID     -\/ ORDER OF DERIVATIVE, ID=0 OR ID=1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01424}01424 \textcolor{comment}{!     KODE   -\/ A PARAMETER TO INDICATE THE SCALING OPTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01425}01425 \textcolor{comment}{!              KODE= 1  RETURNS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01426}01426 \textcolor{comment}{!                       AI=AI(Z)                ON ID=0 OR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01427}01427 \textcolor{comment}{!                       AI=DAI(Z)/DZ            ON ID=1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01428}01428 \textcolor{comment}{!                  = 2  RETURNS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01429}01429 \textcolor{comment}{!                       AI=EXP(ZTA)*AI(Z)       ON ID=0 OR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01430}01430 \textcolor{comment}{!                       AI=EXP(ZTA)*DAI(Z)/DZ   ON ID=1 WHERE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01431}01431 \textcolor{comment}{!                       ZTA=(2/3)*Z*SQRT(Z)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01432}01432 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01433}01433 \textcolor{comment}{!   OUTPUT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01434}01434 \textcolor{comment}{!     AI     -\/ COMPLEX ANSWER DEPENDING ON THE CHOICES FOR ID AND KODE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01435}01435 \textcolor{comment}{!     NZ     -\/ UNDERFLOW INDICATOR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01436}01436 \textcolor{comment}{!              NZ= 0   , NORMAL RETURN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01437}01437 \textcolor{comment}{!              NZ= 1   , AI=CMPLX(0.0,0.0) DUE TO UNDERFLOW IN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01438}01438 \textcolor{comment}{!                        -\/PI/3 < ARG(Z) < PI/3 ON KODE=1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01439}01439 \textcolor{comment}{!     IERR   -\/ ERROR FLAG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01440}01440 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=0, NORMAL RETURN -\/ COMPUTATION COMPLETED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01441}01441 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=1, INPUT ERROR   -\/ NO COMPUTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01442}01442 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=2, OVERFLOW      -\/ NO COMPUTATION, REAL(ZTA)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01443}01443 \textcolor{comment}{!                      TOO LARGE WITH KODE=1.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01444}01444 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=3, ABS(Z) LARGE      -\/ COMPUTATION COMPLETED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01445}01445 \textcolor{comment}{!                      LOSSES OF SIGNIFICANCE BY ARGUMENT REDUCTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01446}01446 \textcolor{comment}{!                      PRODUCE LESS THAN HALF OF MACHINE ACCURACY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01447}01447 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=4, ABS(Z) TOO LARGE  -\/ NO COMPUTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01448}01448 \textcolor{comment}{!                      COMPLETE LOSS OF ACCURACY BY ARGUMENT REDUCTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01449}01449 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=5, ERROR              -\/ NO COMPUTATION,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01450}01450 \textcolor{comment}{!                      ALGORITHM TERMINATION CONDITION NOT MET}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01451}01451 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01452}01452 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01453}01453 \textcolor{comment}{!***LONG DESCRIPTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01454}01454 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01455}01455 \textcolor{comment}{!   AI AND DAI ARE COMPUTED FOR ABS(Z) > 1.0 FROM THE K BESSEL FUNCTIONS BY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01456}01456 \textcolor{comment}{!      AI(Z) = C*SQRT(Z)*K(1/3,ZTA) , DAI(Z) = -\/C*Z*K(2/3,ZTA)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01457}01457 \textcolor{comment}{!                     C = 1.0/(PI*SQRT(3.0))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01458}01458 \textcolor{comment}{!                   ZTA = (2/3)*Z**(3/2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01459}01459 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01460}01460 \textcolor{comment}{!   WITH THE POWER SERIES FOR ABS(Z) <= 1.0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01461}01461 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01462}01462 \textcolor{comment}{!   IN MOST COMPLEX VARIABLE COMPUTATION, ONE MUST EVALUATE ELEMENTARY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01463}01463 \textcolor{comment}{!   FUNCTIONS.  WHEN THE MAGNITUDE OF Z IS LARGE, LOSSES OF SIGNIFICANCE BY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01464}01464 \textcolor{comment}{!   ARGUMENT REDUCTION OCCUR.  CONSEQUENTLY, IF THE MAGNITUDE OF ZETA =}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01465}01465 \textcolor{comment}{!   (2/3)*Z**1.5 EXCEEDS U1 = SQRT(0.5/UR), THEN LOSSES EXCEEDING HALF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01466}01466 \textcolor{comment}{!   PRECISION ARE LIKELY AND AN ERROR FLAG IERR=3 IS TRIGGERED WHERE UR =}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01467}01467 \textcolor{comment}{!   EPSILON(0.0\_dp) = UNIT ROUNDOFF.  ALSO, IF THE MAGNITUDE OF ZETA IS LARGER}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01468}01468 \textcolor{comment}{!   THAN U2=0.5/UR, THEN ALL SIGNIFICANCE IS LOST AND IERR=4.  IN ORDER TO USE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01469}01469 \textcolor{comment}{!   THE INT FUNCTION, ZETA MUST BE FURTHER RESTRICTED NOT TO EXCEED THE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01470}01470 \textcolor{comment}{!   LARGEST INTEGER, U3 = HUGE(0).  THUS, THE MAGNITUDE OF ZETA MUST BE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01471}01471 \textcolor{comment}{!   RESTRICTED BY MIN(U2,U3).  ON 32 BIT MACHINES, U1, U2, AND U3 ARE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01472}01472 \textcolor{comment}{!   APPROXIMATELY 2.0E+3, 4.2E+6, 2.1E+9 IN SINGLE PRECISION ARITHMETIC AND}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01473}01473 \textcolor{comment}{!   1.3E+8, 1.8D+16, 2.1E+9 IN DOUBLE PRECISION ARITHMETIC RESPECTIVELY.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01474}01474 \textcolor{comment}{!   THIS MAKES U2 AND U3 LIMITING IN THEIR RESPECTIVE ARITHMETICS.  THIS MEANS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01475}01475 \textcolor{comment}{!   THAT THE MAGNITUDE OF Z CANNOT EXCEED 3.1E+4 IN SINGLE AND 2.1E+6 IN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01476}01476 \textcolor{comment}{!   DOUBLE PRECISION ARITHMETIC.  THIS ALSO MEANS THAT ONE CAN EXPECT TO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01477}01477 \textcolor{comment}{!   RETAIN, IN THE WORST CASES ON 32 BIT MACHINES, NO DIGITS IN SINGLE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01478}01478 \textcolor{comment}{!   PRECISION AND ONLY 7 DIGITS IN DOUBLE PRECISION ARITHMETIC.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01479}01479 \textcolor{comment}{!   SIMILAR CONSIDERATIONS HOLD FOR OTHER MACHINES.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01480}01480 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01481}01481 \textcolor{comment}{!   THE APPROXIMATE RELATIVE ERROR IN THE MAGNITUDE OF A COMPLEX}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01482}01482 \textcolor{comment}{!   BESSEL FUNCTION CAN BE EXPRESSED BY P*10**S WHERE P = MAX(UNIT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01483}01483 \textcolor{comment}{!   ROUNDOFF,1.0E-\/18) IS THE NOMINAL PRECISION AND 10**S REPRESENTS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01484}01484 \textcolor{comment}{!   THE INCREASE IN ERROR DUE TO ARGUMENT REDUCTION IN THE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01485}01485 \textcolor{comment}{!   ELEMENTARY FUNCTIONS.  HERE, S = MAX(1,ABS(LOG10(ABS(Z))),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01486}01486 \textcolor{comment}{!   ABS(LOG10(FNU))) APPROXIMATELY (I.E. S=MAX(1,ABS(EXPONENT OF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01487}01487 \textcolor{comment}{!   ABS(Z),ABS(EXPONENT OF FNU)) ).  HOWEVER, THE PHASE ANGLE MAY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01488}01488 \textcolor{comment}{!   HAVE ONLY ABSOLUTE ACCURACY.  THIS IS MOST LIKELY TO OCCUR WHEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01489}01489 \textcolor{comment}{!   ONE COMPONENT (IN ABSOLUTE VALUE) IS LARGER THAN THE OTHER BY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01490}01490 \textcolor{comment}{!   SEVERAL ORDERS OF MAGNITUDE.  IF ONE COMPONENT IS 10**K LARGER}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01491}01491 \textcolor{comment}{!   THAN THE OTHER, THEN ONE CAN EXPECT ONLY MAX(ABS(LOG10(P))-\/K,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01492}01492 \textcolor{comment}{!   0) SIGNIFICANT DIGITS; OR, STATED ANOTHER WAY, WHEN K EXCEEDS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01493}01493 \textcolor{comment}{!   THE EXPONENT OF P, NO SIGNIFICANT DIGITS REMAIN IN THE SMALLER}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01494}01494 \textcolor{comment}{!   COMPONENT.  HOWEVER, THE PHASE ANGLE RETAINS ABSOLUTE ACCURACY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01495}01495 \textcolor{comment}{!   BECAUSE, IN COMPLEX ARITHMETIC WITH PRECISION P, THE SMALLER}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01496}01496 \textcolor{comment}{!   COMPONENT WILL NOT (AS A RULE) DECREASE BELOW P TIMES THE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01497}01497 \textcolor{comment}{!   MAGNITUDE OF THE LARGER COMPONENT.  IN THESE EXTREME CASES,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01498}01498 \textcolor{comment}{!   THE PRINCIPAL PHASE ANGLE IS ON THE ORDER OF +P, -\/P, PI/2-\/P, OR -\/PI/2+P.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01499}01499 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01500}01500 \textcolor{comment}{!***REFERENCES  HANDBOOK OF MATHEMATICAL FUNCTIONS BY M. ABRAMOWITZ AND}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01501}01501 \textcolor{comment}{!      I. A. STEGUN, NBS AMS SERIES 55, U.S. DEPT. OF COMMERCE, 1955.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01502}01502 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01503}01503 \textcolor{comment}{!    COMPUTATION OF BESSEL FUNCTIONS OF COMPLEX ARGUMENT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01504}01504 \textcolor{comment}{!      AND LARGE ORDER BY D. E. AMOS, SAND83-\/0643, MAY 1983}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01505}01505 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01506}01506 \textcolor{comment}{!    A SUBROUTINE PACKAGE FOR BESSEL FUNCTIONS OF A COMPLEX ARGUMENT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01507}01507 \textcolor{comment}{!      AND NONNEGATIVE ORDER BY D. E. AMOS, SAND85-\/1018, MAY 1985}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01508}01508 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01509}01509 \textcolor{comment}{!    A PORTABLE PACKAGE FOR BESSEL FUNCTIONS OF A COMPLEX ARGUMENT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01510}01510 \textcolor{comment}{!      AND NONNEGATIVE ORDER BY D. E. AMOS, ACM TRANS. MATH. SOFTWARE,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01511}01511 \textcolor{comment}{!      VOL. 12, NO. 3, SEPTEMBER 1986, PP 265-\/273.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01512}01512 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01513}01513 \textcolor{comment}{!***ROUTINES CALLED  CACAI,CBKNU,I1MACH,R1MACH}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01514}01514 \textcolor{comment}{!***END PROLOGUE  CAIRY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01515}01515 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01516}01516 \textcolor{keywordtype}{COMPLEX (dp)}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{INTENT(IN)}   :: z}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01517}01517 \textcolor{keywordtype}{INTEGER}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{INTENT(IN)}        :: id}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01518}01518 \textcolor{keywordtype}{INTEGER}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{INTENT(IN)}        :: kode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01519}01519 \textcolor{keywordtype}{COMPLEX (dp)}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{INTENT(OUT)}  :: ai}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01522}01522 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01523}01523 \textcolor{keywordtype}{COMPLEX (dp)}  :: csq, cy(1), s1, s2, trm1, trm2, zta, z3}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01524}01524 real(dp)     :: aa, ad, ak, alim, atrm, az, az3, bk, ck, dig, dk, d1, d2, \&}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01525}01525                  elim, fid, fnu, rl, r1m5, sfac, tol, zi, zr, z3i, z3r, bb, \&}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01526}01526                  alaz}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01527}01527 \textcolor{keywordtype}{INTEGER}       :: iflag, k, k1, k2, mr, nn}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01528}01528 real(dp), \textcolor{keywordtype}{PARAMETER}  :: tth = 6.66666666666666667d-\/01,  \&}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01529}01529            c1 = 3.55028053887817240d-\/01, c2 = 2.58819403792806799d-\/01,  \&}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01530}01530            coef = 1.83776298473930683d-\/01}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01531}01531 \textcolor{keywordtype}{COMPLEX (dp)}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{PARAMETER}  :: cone = (1.0\_dp, 0.0\_dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01532}01532 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01533}01533 \textcolor{comment}{!***FIRST EXECUTABLE STATEMENT  CAIRY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01534}01534 ierr = 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01535}01535 nz = 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01536}01536 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (id < 0 .OR. id > 1) ierr = 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01537}01537 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (kode < 1 .OR. kode > 2) ierr = 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01538}01538 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (ierr /= 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{RETURN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01539}01539 az = abs(z)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01680}01680       iflag = 2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01681}01681       sfac = 1.0\_dp / tol}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01682}01682       \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (aa < -\/elim) \textcolor{keywordflow}{GO TO} 40}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01683}01683 \textcolor{keywordflow}{    END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01684}01684 \textcolor{keywordflow}{  END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01685}01685   \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }cbknu(zta, fnu, kode, 1, cy, nz, tol, elim, alim)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01686}01686 \textcolor{keywordflow}{END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01687}01687 s1 = cy(1) * coef}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01688}01688 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (iflag == 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01689}01689   \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (id /= 1) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01690}01690     ai = csq * s1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01691}01691     \textcolor{keywordflow}{RETURN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01692}01692 \textcolor{keywordflow}{  END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01693}01693   ai = -\/z * s1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01694}01694   \textcolor{keywordflow}{RETURN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01695}01695 \textcolor{keywordflow}{END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01696}01696 s1 = s1 * sfac}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01697}01697 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (id /= 1) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01698}01698   s1 = s1 * csq}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01699}01699   ai = s1 / sfac}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01701}01701 \textcolor{keywordflow}{END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01702}01702 s1 = -\/s1 * z}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01703}01703 ai = s1 / sfac}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01704}01704 \textcolor{keywordflow}{RETURN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01705}01705 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01706}01706 30 aa = 1.0e+3 * tiny(0.0\_dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01707}01707 s1 = cmplx(0.0\_dp, 0.0\_dp, kind=dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01708}01708 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (id /= 1) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01736}01736 }
