\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01738}01738 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01739}01739 \textcolor{keyword}{SUBROUTINE }cbiry(z, id, kode, bi, ierr)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01740}01740 \textcolor{comment}{!***BEGIN PROLOGUE  CBIRY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01741}01741 \textcolor{comment}{!***DATE WRITTEN   830501   (YYMMDD)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01742}01742 \textcolor{comment}{!***REVISION DATE  890801, 930101   (YYMMDD)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01743}01743 \textcolor{comment}{!***CATEGORY NO.  B5K}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01744}01744 \textcolor{comment}{!***KEYWORDS  AIRY FUNCTION,BESSEL FUNCTIONS OF ORDER ONE THIRD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01745}01745 \textcolor{comment}{!***AUTHOR  AMOS, DONALD E., SANDIA NATIONAL LABORATORIES}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01746}01746 \textcolor{comment}{!***PURPOSE  TO COMPUTE AIRY FUNCTIONS BI(Z) AND DBI(Z) FOR COMPLEX Z}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01747}01747 \textcolor{comment}{!***DESCRIPTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01748}01748 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01749}01749 \textcolor{comment}{!   ON KODE=1, CBIRY COMPUTES THE COMPLEX AIRY FUNCTION BI(Z) OR ITS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01750}01750 \textcolor{comment}{!   DERIVATIVE DBI(Z)/DZ ON ID=0 OR ID=1 RESPECTIVELY.  ON KODE=2,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01751}01751 \textcolor{comment}{!   A SCALING OPTION EXP(-\/AXZTA)*BI(Z) OR EXP(-\/AXZTA)*DBI(Z)/DZ}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01752}01752 \textcolor{comment}{!   IS PROVIDED TO REMOVE THE EXPONENTIAL BEHAVIOR IN BOTH THE LEFT AND}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01753}01753 \textcolor{comment}{!   RIGHT HALF PLANES WHERE ZTA = (2/3)*Z*SQRT(Z) = CMPLX(XZTA,YZTA)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01754}01754 \textcolor{comment}{!   AND AXZTA=ABS(XZTA).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01755}01755 \textcolor{comment}{!   DEFINITIONS AND NOTATION ARE FOUND IN THE NBS HANDBOOK OF MATHEMATICAL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01756}01756 \textcolor{comment}{!   FUNCTIONS (REF. 1).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01757}01757 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01758}01758 \textcolor{comment}{!   INPUT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01759}01759 \textcolor{comment}{!     Z      -\/ Z=CMPLX(X,Y)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01760}01760 \textcolor{comment}{!     ID     -\/ ORDER OF DERIVATIVE, ID=0 OR ID=1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01761}01761 \textcolor{comment}{!     KODE   -\/ A PARAMETER TO INDICATE THE SCALING OPTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01762}01762 \textcolor{comment}{!              KODE= 1  RETURNS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01763}01763 \textcolor{comment}{!                       BI=BI(Z)                 ON ID=0 OR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01764}01764 \textcolor{comment}{!                       BI=DBI(Z)/DZ             ON ID=1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01765}01765 \textcolor{comment}{!                  = 2  RETURNS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01766}01766 \textcolor{comment}{!                       BI=EXP(-\/AXZTA)*BI(Z)     ON ID=0 OR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01767}01767 \textcolor{comment}{!                       BI=EXP(-\/AXZTA)*DBI(Z)/DZ ON ID=1 WHERE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01768}01768 \textcolor{comment}{!                       ZTA=(2/3)*Z*SQRT(Z)=CMPLX(XZTA,YZTA)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01769}01769 \textcolor{comment}{!                       AND AXZTA=ABS(XZTA)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01770}01770 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01771}01771 \textcolor{comment}{!   OUTPUT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01772}01772 \textcolor{comment}{!     BI     -\/ COMPLEX ANSWER DEPENDING ON THE CHOICES FOR ID AND KODE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01773}01773 \textcolor{comment}{!     IERR   -\/ ERROR FLAG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01774}01774 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=0, NORMAL RETURN -\/ COMPUTATION COMPLETED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01775}01775 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=1, INPUT ERROR   -\/ NO COMPUTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01776}01776 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=2, OVERFLOW      -\/ NO COMPUTATION, REAL(Z)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01777}01777 \textcolor{comment}{!                      TOO LARGE WITH KODE=1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01778}01778 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=3, ABS(Z) LARGE      -\/ COMPUTATION COMPLETED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01779}01779 \textcolor{comment}{!                      LOSSES OF SIGNIFICANCE BY ARGUMENT REDUCTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01780}01780 \textcolor{comment}{!                      PRODUCE LESS THAN HALF OF MACHINE ACCURACY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01781}01781 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=4, ABS(Z) TOO LARGE  -\/ NO COMPUTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01782}01782 \textcolor{comment}{!                      COMPLETE LOSS OF ACCURACY BY ARGUMENT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01783}01783 \textcolor{comment}{!                      REDUCTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01784}01784 \textcolor{comment}{!              IERR=5, ERROR              -\/ NO COMPUTATION,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01785}01785 \textcolor{comment}{!                      ALGORITHM TERMINATION CONDITION NOT MET}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01786}01786 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01787}01787 \textcolor{comment}{!***LONG DESCRIPTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01788}01788 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01789}01789 \textcolor{comment}{!      BI AND DBI ARE COMPUTED FOR ABS(Z) > 1.0 FROM THE I BESSEL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01790}01790 \textcolor{comment}{!      FUNCTIONS BY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01791}01791 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01792}01792 \textcolor{comment}{!             BI(Z)=C*SQRT(Z)*( I(-\/1/3,ZTA) + I(1/3,ZTA) )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01793}01793 \textcolor{comment}{!            DBI(Z)=C *  Z  * ( I(-\/2/3,ZTA) + I(2/3,ZTA) )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01794}01794 \textcolor{comment}{!                            C=1.0/SQRT(3.0)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01795}01795 \textcolor{comment}{!                            ZTA=(2/3)*Z**(3/2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01796}01796 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01797}01797 \textcolor{comment}{!      WITH THE POWER SERIES FOR ABS(Z) <= 1.0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01798}01798 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01799}01799 \textcolor{comment}{!      IN MOST COMPLEX VARIABLE COMPUTATION, ONE MUST EVALUATE ELE-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01800}01800 \textcolor{comment}{!      MENTARY FUNCTIONS. WHEN THE MAGNITUDE OF Z IS LARGE, LOSSES}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01801}01801 \textcolor{comment}{!      OF SIGNIFICANCE BY ARGUMENT REDUCTION OCCUR. CONSEQUENTLY, IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01802}01802 \textcolor{comment}{!      THE MAGNITUDE OF ZETA=(2/3)*Z**1.5 EXCEEDS U1=SQRT(0.5/UR),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01803}01803 \textcolor{comment}{!      THEN LOSSES EXCEEDING HALF PRECISION ARE LIKELY AND AN ERROR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01804}01804 \textcolor{comment}{!      FLAG IERR=3 IS TRIGGERED WHERE UR=EPSILON(0.0\_dp)=UNIT ROUNDOFF.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01805}01805 \textcolor{comment}{!      ALSO, IF THE MAGNITUDE OF ZETA IS LARGER THAN U2=0.5/UR, THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01806}01806 \textcolor{comment}{!      ALL SIGNIFICANCE IS LOST AND IERR=4. IN ORDER TO USE THE INT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01807}01807 \textcolor{comment}{!      FUNCTION, ZETA MUST BE FURTHER RESTRICTED NOT TO EXCEED THE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01808}01808 \textcolor{comment}{!      LARGEST INTEGER, U3=HUGE(0). THUS, THE MAGNITUDE OF ZETA}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01809}01809 \textcolor{comment}{!      MUST BE RESTRICTED BY MIN(U2,U3). ON 32 BIT MACHINES, U1,U2,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01810}01810 \textcolor{comment}{!      AND U3 ARE APPROXIMATELY 2.0E+3, 4.2E+6, 2.1E+9 IN SINGLE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01811}01811 \textcolor{comment}{!      PRECISION ARITHMETIC AND 1.3E+8, 1.8D+16, 2.1E+9 IN DOUBLE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01812}01812 \textcolor{comment}{!      PRECISION ARITHMETIC RESPECTIVELY. THIS MAKES U2 AND U3 LIMIT-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01813}01813 \textcolor{comment}{!      ING IN THEIR RESPECTIVE ARITHMETICS. THIS MEANS THAT THE MAG-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01814}01814 \textcolor{comment}{!      NITUDE OF Z CANNOT EXCEED 3.1E+4 IN SINGLE AND 2.1E+6 IN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01815}01815 \textcolor{comment}{!      DOUBLE PRECISION ARITHMETIC. THIS ALSO MEANS THAT ONE CAN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01816}01816 \textcolor{comment}{!      EXPECT TO RETAIN, IN THE WORST CASES ON 32 BIT MACHINES,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01817}01817 \textcolor{comment}{!      NO DIGITS IN SINGLE PRECISION AND ONLY 7 DIGITS IN DOUBLE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01818}01818 \textcolor{comment}{!      PRECISION ARITHMETIC.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01819}01819 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01820}01820 \textcolor{comment}{!      THE APPROXIMATE RELATIVE ERROR IN THE MAGNITUDE OF A COMPLEX}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01821}01821 \textcolor{comment}{!      BESSEL FUNCTION CAN BE EXPRESSED BY P*10**S WHERE P=MAX(UNIT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01822}01822 \textcolor{comment}{!      ROUNDOFF,1.0E-\/18) IS THE NOMINAL PRECISION AND 10**S REPRE-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01823}01823 \textcolor{comment}{!      SENTS THE INCREASE IN ERROR DUE TO ARGUMENT REDUCTION IN THE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01824}01824 \textcolor{comment}{!      ELEMENTARY FUNCTIONS. HERE, S=MAX(1,ABS(LOG10(ABS(Z))),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01825}01825 \textcolor{comment}{!      ABS(LOG10(FNU))) APPROXIMATELY (I.E. S=MAX(1,ABS(EXPONENT OF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01826}01826 \textcolor{comment}{!      ABS(Z),ABS(EXPONENT OF FNU)) ). HOWEVER, THE PHASE ANGLE MAY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01827}01827 \textcolor{comment}{!      HAVE ONLY ABSOLUTE ACCURACY. THIS IS MOST LIKELY TO OCCUR WHEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01828}01828 \textcolor{comment}{!      ONE COMPONENT (IN ABSOLUTE VALUE) IS LARGER THAN THE OTHER BY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01829}01829 \textcolor{comment}{!      SEVERAL ORDERS OF MAGNITUDE. IF ONE COMPONENT IS 10**K LARGER}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01830}01830 \textcolor{comment}{!      THAN THE OTHER, THEN ONE CAN EXPECT ONLY MAX(ABS(LOG10(P))-\/K,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01831}01831 \textcolor{comment}{!      0) SIGNIFICANT DIGITS; OR, STATED ANOTHER WAY, WHEN K EXCEEDS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01832}01832 \textcolor{comment}{!      THE EXPONENT OF P, NO SIGNIFICANT DIGITS REMAIN IN THE SMALLER}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01833}01833 \textcolor{comment}{!      COMPONENT. HOWEVER, THE PHASE ANGLE RETAINS ABSOLUTE ACCURACY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01834}01834 \textcolor{comment}{!      BECAUSE, IN COMPLEX ARITHMETIC WITH PRECISION P, THE SMALLER}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01835}01835 \textcolor{comment}{!      COMPONENT WILL NOT (AS A RULE) DECREASE BELOW P TIMES THE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01836}01836 \textcolor{comment}{!      MAGNITUDE OF THE LARGER COMPONENT. IN THESE EXTREME CASES,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01837}01837 \textcolor{comment}{!      THE PRINCIPAL PHASE ANGLE IS ON THE ORDER OF +P, -\/P, PI/2-\/P,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01838}01838 \textcolor{comment}{!      OR -\/PI/2+P.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01839}01839 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01840}01840 \textcolor{comment}{!***REFERENCES  HANDBOOK OF MATHEMATICAL FUNCTIONS BY M. ABRAMOWITZ AND}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01841}01841 \textcolor{comment}{!           I. A. STEGUN, NBS AMS SERIES 55, U.S. DEPT. OF COMMERCE, 1955.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01842}01842 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01843}01843 \textcolor{comment}{!         COMPUTATION OF BESSEL FUNCTIONS OF COMPLEX ARGUMENT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01844}01844 \textcolor{comment}{!           AND LARGE ORDER BY D. E. AMOS, SAND83-\/0643, MAY 1983}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01845}01845 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01846}01846 \textcolor{comment}{!         A SUBROUTINE PACKAGE FOR BESSEL FUNCTIONS OF A COMPLEX ARGUMENT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l01847}01847 \textcolor{comment}{!           AND NONNEGATIVE ORDER BY D. E. AMOS, SAND85-\/1018, MAY 1985}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02211}02211 \textcolor{keyword}{SUBROUTINE }cuoik(z, fnu, kode, ikflg, n, y, nuf, tol, elim, alim)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02212}02212 \textcolor{comment}{!***BEGIN PROLOGUE  CUOIK}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02213}02213 \textcolor{comment}{!***REFER TO  CBESI,CBESK,CBESH}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02214}02214 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02215}02215 \textcolor{comment}{!   CUOIK COMPUTES THE LEADING TERMS OF THE UNIFORM ASYMPTOTIC EXPANSIONS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02216}02216 \textcolor{comment}{!   FOR THE I AND K FUNCTIONS AND COMPARES THEM (IN LOGARITHMIC FORM)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02217}02217 \textcolor{comment}{!   TO ALIM AND ELIM FOR OVER AND UNDERFLOW, WHERE ALIM < ELIM.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02218}02218 \textcolor{comment}{!   IF THE MAGNITUDE, BASED ON THE LEADING EXPONENTIAL, IS LESS THAN ALIM OR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02219}02219 \textcolor{comment}{!   GREATER THAN -\/ALIM, THEN THE RESULT IS ON SCALE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02220}02220 \textcolor{comment}{!   IF NOT, THEN A REFINED TEST USING OTHER MULTIPLIERS (IN LOGARITHMIC FORM)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02221}02221 \textcolor{comment}{!   IS MADE BASED ON ELIM.  HERE EXP(-\/ELIM) = SMALLEST MACHINE NUMBER*1000}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02222}02222 \textcolor{comment}{!   AND EXP(-\/ALIM) = EXP(-\/ELIM)/TOL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02223}02223 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02224}02224 \textcolor{comment}{!   IKFLG=1 MEANS THE I SEQUENCE IS TESTED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02225}02225 \textcolor{comment}{!        =2 MEANS THE K SEQUENCE IS TESTED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02226}02226 \textcolor{comment}{!   NUF = 0 MEANS THE LAST MEMBER OF THE SEQUENCE IS ON SCALE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02227}02227 \textcolor{comment}{!       =-\/1 MEANS AN OVERFLOW WOULD OCCUR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02228}02228 \textcolor{comment}{!   IKFLG=1 AND NUF > 0 MEANS THE LAST NUF Y VALUES WERE SET TO ZERO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02229}02229 \textcolor{comment}{!           THE FIRST N-\/NUF VALUES MUST BE SET BY ANOTHER ROUTINE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02230}02230 \textcolor{comment}{!   IKFLG=2 AND NUF = N MEANS ALL Y VALUES WERE SET TO ZERO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02231}02231 \textcolor{comment}{!   IKFLG=2 AND 0 < NUF < N NOT CONSIDERED.  Y MUST BE SET BY ANOTHER ROUTINE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02232}02232 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02443}02443 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02444}02444 \textcolor{comment}{!     CINU=CINU*(CONJG(CT)/ABS(CT))*(1.0\_dp/ABS(CT) PREVENTS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02445}02445 \textcolor{comment}{!     UNDER-\/ OR OVERFLOW PREMATURELY BY SQUARING ABS(CT)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02446}02446 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02447}02447   ct = zr * (c2 + st*c1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02448}02448   act = abs(ct)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02449}02449   rct = cmplx(1.0\_dp/act, 0.0\_dp, kind=dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02450}02450   ct = conjg(ct) * rct}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02451}02451   cinu = cinu * rct * ct}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02452}02452   y(1) = cinu * cscl}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02453}02453   \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (n == 1) \textcolor{keywordflow}{RETURN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02454}02454   \textcolor{keywordflow}{DO}  i = 2, n}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02455}02455     cinu = st * cinu}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02456}02456     st = y(i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02457}02457     y(i) = cinu * cscl}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02458}02458 \textcolor{keywordflow}{  END DO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02459}02459   \textcolor{keywordflow}{RETURN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02460}02460 \textcolor{keywordflow}{END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02461}02461 nz = -\/1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02462}02462 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (nw == -\/2) nz = -\/2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02463}02463 \textcolor{keywordflow}{RETURN}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02487}02487 real(dp)     :: ack, ak, ap, at, az, bk, fkap, fkk, flam, fnf, rho,  \&}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02492}02492                             ctwo = (2.0\_dp,0.0\_dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02493}02493 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02494}02494 scle = 1.0e+3 * tiny(0.0\_dp) / tol}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02495}02495 nz = 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02496}02496 az = abs(z)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02497}02497 x = real(z, kind=dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02498}02498 iaz = az}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02499}02499 ifnu = fnu}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02500}02500 inu = ifnu + n -\/ 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02501}02501 at = iaz + 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02502}02502 ck = cmplx(at, 0.0\_dp, kind=dp) / z}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02503}02503 rz = ctwo / z}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02504}02504 p1 = czero}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02505}02505 p2 = cone}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02506}02506 ack = (at + 1.0\_dp) / az}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02507}02507 rho = ack + sqrt(ack*ack -\/ 1.0\_dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02508}02508 rho2 = rho * rho}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02509}02509 tst = (rho2+rho2) / ((rho2-\/1.0\_dp)*(rho-\/1.0\_dp))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02510}02510 tst = tst / tol}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02511}02511 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02512}02512 \textcolor{comment}{!     COMPUTE RELATIVE TRUNCATION ERROR INDEX FOR SERIES}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02513}02513 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02514}02514 ak = at}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02515}02515 \textcolor{keywordflow}{DO}  i = 1, 80}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02516}02516   pt = p2}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02518}02518   p1 = pt}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02519}02519   ck = ck + rz}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02520}02520   ap = abs(p2)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02521}02521   \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (ap > tst*ak*ak) \textcolor{keywordflow}{GO TO} 20}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02522}02522   ak = ak + 1.0\_dp}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02523}02523 \textcolor{keywordflow}{END DO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02524}02524 \textcolor{keywordflow}{GO TO} 90}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02525}02525 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02526}02526 20 i = i + 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02527}02527 k = 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02528}02528 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (inu >= iaz) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02529}02529 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02530}02530 \textcolor{comment}{!     COMPUTE RELATIVE TRUNCATION ERROR FOR RATIOS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02531}02531 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02532}02532   p1 = czero}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02533}02533   p2 = cone}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02534}02534   at = inu + 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02535}02535   ck = cmplx(at, 0.0\_dp, kind=dp) / z}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02536}02536   ack = at / az}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02537}02537   tst = sqrt(ack/tol)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02538}02538   itime = 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02539}02539   \textcolor{keywordflow}{DO}  k = 1, 80}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02541}02541     p2 = p1 -\/ ck * p2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02542}02542     p1 = pt}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02543}02543     ck = ck + rz}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02545}02545     \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (ap >= tst) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02546}02546       \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (itime == 2) \textcolor{keywordflow}{GO TO} 40}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02547}02547       ack = abs(ck)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02548}02548       flam = ack + sqrt(ack*ack -\/ 1.0\_dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02549}02549       fkap = ap / abs(p1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02550}02550       rho = min(flam,fkap)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02551}02551       tst = tst * sqrt(rho/(rho*rho -\/ 1.0\_dp))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02552}02552       itime = 2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02553}02553 \textcolor{keywordflow}{    END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02554}02554 \textcolor{keywordflow}{  END DO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02555}02555   \textcolor{keywordflow}{GO TO} 90}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02556}02556 \textcolor{keywordflow}{END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02557}02557 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02558}02558 \textcolor{comment}{!     BACKWARD RECURRENCE AND SUM NORMALIZING RELATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02559}02559 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02560}02560 40 k = k + 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02561}02561 kk = max(i+iaz, k+inu)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02562}02562 fkk = kk}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02563}02563 p1 = czero}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02564}02564 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02565}02565 \textcolor{comment}{!     SCALE P2 AND SUM BY SCLE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02566}02566 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02567}02567 p2 = cmplx(scle, 0.0\_dp, kind=dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02568}02568 fnf = fnu -\/ ifnu}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02569}02569 tfnf = fnf + fnf}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02570}02570 bk = gamln(fkk+tfnf+1.0\_dp) -\/ gamln(fkk+1.0\_dp) -\/ gamln(tfnf+1.0\_dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02571}02571 bk = exp(bk)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02572}02572 sum = czero}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02573}02573 km = kk -\/ inu}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02574}02574 \textcolor{keywordflow}{DO}  i = 1, km}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02575}02575   pt = p2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02576}02576   p2 = p1 + cmplx(fkk+fnf, 0.0\_dp, kind=dp) * rz * p2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02577}02577   p1 = pt}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02578}02578   ak = 1.0\_dp -\/ tfnf / (fkk+tfnf)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02579}02579   ack = bk * ak}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02580}02580   sum = sum + cmplx(ack+bk, 0.0\_dp, kind=dp) * p1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02581}02581   bk = ack}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02582}02582   fkk = fkk -\/ 1.0\_dp}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02583}02583 \textcolor{keywordflow}{END DO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02584}02584 y(n) = p2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02585}02585 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (n /= 1) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02586}02586   \textcolor{keywordflow}{DO}  i = 2, n}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02587}02587     pt = p2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02588}02588     p2 = p1 + cmplx(fkk+fnf, 0.0\_dp, kind=dp) * rz * p2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02589}02589     p1 = pt}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02590}02590     ak = 1.0\_dp -\/ tfnf / (fkk+tfnf)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02591}02591     ack = bk * ak}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02592}02592     sum = sum + cmplx(ack+bk, 0.0\_dp, kind=dp) * p1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02593}02593     bk = ack}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02594}02594     fkk = fkk -\/ 1.0\_dp}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02595}02595     m = n -\/ i + 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02596}02596     y(m) = p2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02597}02597 \textcolor{keywordflow}{  END DO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02598}02598 \textcolor{keywordflow}{END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02599}02599 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (ifnu > 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02600}02600   \textcolor{keywordflow}{DO}  i = 1, ifnu}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02601}02601     pt = p2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02602}02602     p2 = p1 + cmplx(fkk+fnf, 0.0\_dp, kind=dp) * rz * p2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02603}02603     p1 = pt}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02604}02604     ak = 1.0\_dp -\/ tfnf / (fkk+tfnf)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02605}02605     ack = bk * ak}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02606}02606     sum = sum + cmplx(ack+bk, 0.0\_dp, kind=dp) * p1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02607}02607     bk = ack}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02608}02608     fkk = fkk -\/ 1.0\_dp}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02609}02609 \textcolor{keywordflow}{  END DO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02610}02610 \textcolor{keywordflow}{END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02611}02611 pt = z}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02612}02612 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (kode == 2) pt = pt -\/ x}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02613}02613 p1 = -\/fnf * log(rz) + pt}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02614}02614 ap = gamln(1.0\_dp+fnf)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02615}02615 pt = p1 -\/ ap}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02616}02616 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02617}02617 \textcolor{comment}{!     THE DIVISION EXP(PT)/(SUM+P2) IS ALTERED TO AVOID OVERFLOW}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02618}02618 \textcolor{comment}{!     IN THE DENOMINATOR BY SQUARING LARGE QUANTITIES}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02619}02619 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02620}02620 p2 = p2 + sum}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02621}02621 ap = abs(p2)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02622}02622 p1 = cmplx(1.0\_dp/ap, 0.0\_dp, kind=dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02623}02623 ck = exp(pt) * p1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02624}02624 pt = conjg(p2) * p1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02625}02625 cnorm = ck * pt}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02626}02626 y(1:n) = y(1:n) * cnorm}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02627}02627 \textcolor{keywordflow}{RETURN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02628}02628 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02629}02629 90 nz = -\/2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02630}02630 \textcolor{keywordflow}{RETURN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02631}02631 \textcolor{keyword}{END SUBROUTINE }cmlri}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02646}02646 \textcolor{comment}{!  ABSTRACT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02647}02647 \textcolor{comment}{!      CUNHJ COMPUTES PARAMETERS FOR BESSEL FUNCTIONS C(FNU,Z) =}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02648}02648 \textcolor{comment}{!      J(FNU,Z), Y(FNU,Z) OR H(I,FNU,Z) I=1,2 FOR LARGE ORDERS FNU}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02649}02649 \textcolor{comment}{!      BY MEANS OF THE UNIFORM ASYMPTOTIC EXPANSION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02650}02650 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02651}02651 \textcolor{comment}{!      C(FNU,Z) = C1*PHI*( ASUM*AIRY(ARG) + C2*BSUM*DAIRY(ARG) )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02652}02652 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02653}02653 \textcolor{comment}{!      FOR PROPER CHOICES OF C1, C2, AIRY AND DAIRY WHERE AIRY IS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02654}02654 \textcolor{comment}{!      AN AIRY FUNCTION AND DAIRY IS ITS DERIVATIVE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02655}02655 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02656}02656 \textcolor{comment}{!            (2/3)*FNU*ZETA**1.5 = ZETA1-\/ZETA2,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02657}02657 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02658}02658 \textcolor{comment}{!      ZETA1 = 0.5*FNU*LOG((1+W)/(1-\/W)), ZETA2 = FNU*W FOR SCALING}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02659}02659 \textcolor{comment}{!      PURPOSES IN AIRY FUNCTIONS FROM CAIRY OR CBIRY.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02660}02660 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02661}02661 \textcolor{comment}{!      MCONJ = SIGN OF AIMAG(Z), BUT IS AMBIGUOUS WHEN Z IS REAL AND}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02662}02662 \textcolor{comment}{!      MUST BE SPECIFIED.  IPMTR=0 RETURNS ALL PARAMETERS.  IPMTR =}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l02663}02663 \textcolor{comment}{!      1 COMPUTES ALL EXCEPT ASUM AND BSUM.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l03003}03003           m = l2 + k}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l03004}03004           sumb = sumb + p(k) * beta(m)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l03005}03005           \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (ap(k) < atol) \textcolor{keywordflow}{EXIT}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l03009}03009 \textcolor{keywordflow}{      END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l03010}03010       \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (ias == 1 .AND. ibs == 1) \textcolor{keywordflow}{EXIT}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l03015}03015 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l03016}03016   asum = asum + cone}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l03017}03017   pp = rfnu * rfn13}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l03144}03144 \textcolor{keyword}{SUBROUTINE }cseri(z, fnu, kode, n, y, nz, tol, elim, alim)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l03145}03145 \textcolor{comment}{!***BEGIN PROLOGUE  CSERI}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l03146}03146 \textcolor{comment}{!***REFER TO  CBESI,CBESK}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l03147}03147 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l03148}03148 \textcolor{comment}{!     CSERI COMPUTES THE I BESSEL FUNCTION FOR REAL(Z) >= 0.0 BY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l03149}03149 \textcolor{comment}{!     MEANS OF THE POWER SERIES FOR LARGE ABS(Z) IN THE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l03150}03150 \textcolor{comment}{!     REGION ABS(Z) <= 2*SQRT(FNU+1). NZ=0 IS A NORMAL RETURN.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l03151}03151 \textcolor{comment}{!     NZ > 0 MEANS THAT THE LAST NZ COMPONENTS WERE SET TO ZERO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l03152}03152 \textcolor{comment}{!     DUE TO UNDERFLOW. NZ < 0 MEANS UNDERFLOW OCCURRED, BUT THE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l03153}03153 \textcolor{comment}{!     CONDITION ABS(Z) <= 2*SQRT(FNU+1) WAS VIOLATED AND THE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l03154}03154 \textcolor{comment}{!     COMPUTATION MUST BE COMPLETED IN ANOTHER ROUTINE WITH N=N-\/ABS(NZ).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l03155}03155 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l03156}03156 \textcolor{comment}{!***ROUTINES CALLED  CUCHK,GAMLN,R1MACH}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l03157}03157 \textcolor{comment}{!***END PROLOGUE  CSERI}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04548}04548 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (nd > 2) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04550}04550   bry(2) = 1.0\_dp / bry(1)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04556}04556   k = nd -\/ 2}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04576}04576         s2 = c2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04577}04577         s1 = s1 * css(iflag)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04578}04578         s2 = s2 * css(iflag)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04579}04579         c1 = csr(iflag)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04580}04580 \textcolor{keywordflow}{      END IF}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04621}04621 \textcolor{comment}{!     CUNI2 COMPUTES I(FNU,Z) IN THE RIGHT HALF PLANE BY MEANS OF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04622}04622 \textcolor{comment}{!     UNIFORM ASYMPTOTIC EXPANSION FOR J(FNU,ZN) WHERE ZN IS Z*I}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04625}04625 \textcolor{comment}{!     FNUL IS THE SMALLEST ORDER PERMITTED FOR THE ASYMPTOTIC}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04626}04626 \textcolor{comment}{!     EXPANSION.  NLAST=0 MEANS ALL OF THE Y VALUES WERE SET.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04627}04627 \textcolor{comment}{!     NLAST.NE.0 IS THE NUMBER LEFT TO BE COMPUTED BY ANOTHER}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04628}04628 \textcolor{comment}{!     FORMULA FOR ORDERS FNU TO FNU+NLAST-\/1 BECAUSE FNU+NLAST-\/1 < FNUL.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04629}04629 \textcolor{comment}{!     Y(I) = CZERO FOR I=NLAST+1,N}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04711}04711 10 nn = min(2,nd)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04881}04881     aln = -\/xx -\/ xx + log(as1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04882}04882     s1d = s1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04883}04883     s1 = czero}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04887}04887       s1 = exp(c1)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04889}04889       iuf = iuf + 1}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04961}04961 real(dp), \textcolor{keywordtype}{PARAMETER}  :: czero = (0.0\_dp,0.0\_dp), cone = (1.0\_dp,0.0\_dp)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04973}04973 rz = (cone+cone) / z}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04974}04974 t1 = fnup * rz}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04975}04975 p2 = -\/t1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04976}04976 p1 = cone}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04977}04977 t1 = t1 + rz}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04978}04978 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (id > 0) id = 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04979}04979 ap2 = abs(p2)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04980}04980 ap1 = abs(p1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04981}04981 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04982}04982 \textcolor{comment}{!     THE OVERFLOW TEST ON K(FNU+I-\/1,Z) BEFORE THE CALL TO CBKNX}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04983}04983 \textcolor{comment}{!     GUARANTEES THAT P2 IS ON SCALE. SCALE TEST1 AND ALL SUBSEQUENT P2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04984}04984 \textcolor{comment}{!     VALUES BY AP1 TO ENSURE THAT AN OVERFLOW DOES NOT OCCUR PREMATURELY.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04985}04985 \textcolor{comment}{!-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04986}04986 arg = (ap2+ap2) / (ap1*tol)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04987}04987 test1 = sqrt(arg)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04988}04988 test = test1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04989}04989 rap1 = 1.0\_dp / ap1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04990}04990 p1 = p1 * rap1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04991}04991 p2 = p2 * rap1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04992}04992 ap2 = ap2 * rap1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04993}04993 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04994}04994 10 k = k + 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04995}04995 ap1 = ap2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04996}04996 pt = p2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04997}04997 p2 = p1 -\/ t1 * p2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04998}04998 p1 = pt}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l04999}04999 t1 = t1 + rz}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05000}05000 ap2 = abs(p2)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05001}05001 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (ap1 <= test) \textcolor{keywordflow}{GO TO} 10}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05002}05002 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (itime /= 2) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05003}05003   ak = abs(t1) * 0.5\_dp}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05004}05004   flam = ak + sqrt(ak*ak -\/ 1.0\_dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05005}05005   rho = min(ap2/ap1, flam)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05006}05006   test = test1 * sqrt(rho/(rho*rho -\/ 1.0\_dp))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05007}05007   itime = 2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05008}05008   \textcolor{keywordflow}{GO TO} 10}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05009}05009 \textcolor{keywordflow}{END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05010}05010 kk = k + 1 -\/ id}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05011}05011 ak = kk}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05012}05012 dfnu = fnu + (n-\/1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05013}05013 cdfnu = dfnu}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05014}05014 t1 = ak}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05015}05015 p1 = 1.0\_dp/ap2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05016}05016 p2 = czero}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05017}05017 \textcolor{keywordflow}{DO}  i = 1, kk}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05018}05018   pt = p1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05019}05019   p1 = rz * (cdfnu+t1) * p1 + p2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05020}05020   p2 = pt}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05021}05021   t1 = t1 -\/ cone}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05022}05022 \textcolor{keywordflow}{END DO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05023}05023 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (real(p1, kind=dp) == 0.0\_dp .AND. aimag(p1) == 0.0\_dp) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05024}05024   p1 = cmplx(tol, tol, kind=dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05025}05025 \textcolor{keywordflow}{END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05026}05026 cy(n) = p2 / p1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05027}05027 \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (n == 1) \textcolor{keywordflow}{RETURN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05028}05028 k = n -\/ 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05029}05029 ak = k}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05030}05030 t1 = ak}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05031}05031 cdfnu = fnu * rz}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05032}05032 \textcolor{keywordflow}{DO}  i = 2, n}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05033}05033   pt = cdfnu + t1 * rz + cy(k+1)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05036}05036 \textcolor{keywordflow}{  END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05037}05037   cy(k) = cone / pt}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05038}05038   t1 = t1 -\/ cone}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05039}05039   k = k -\/ 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05040}05040 \textcolor{keywordflow}{END DO}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05923}05923 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05924}05924 \textcolor{comment}{!   GAMLN COMPUTES THE NATURAL LOG OF THE GAMMA FUNCTION FOR Z > 0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05925}05925 \textcolor{comment}{!   THE ASYMPTOTIC EXPANSION IS USED TO GENERATE VALUES GREATER THAN ZMIN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05926}05926 \textcolor{comment}{!   WHICH ARE ADJUSTED BY THE RECURSION G(Z+1)=Z*G(Z) FOR Z <= ZMIN.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05927}05927 \textcolor{comment}{!   THE FUNCTION WAS MADE AS PORTABLE AS POSSIBLE BY COMPUTIMG ZMIN FROM THE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05928}05928 \textcolor{comment}{!   NUMBER OF BASE 10 DIGITS IN A WORD,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05929}05929 \textcolor{comment}{!   RLN = MAX(-\/LOG10(EPSILON(0.0\_dp)), 0.5E-\/18)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05930}05930 \textcolor{comment}{!   LIMITED TO 18 DIGITS OF (RELATIVE) ACCURACY.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05931}05931 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05932}05932 \textcolor{comment}{!   SINCE INTEGER ARGUMENTS ARE COMMON, A TABLE LOOK UP ON 100}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05933}05933 \textcolor{comment}{!   VALUES IS USED FOR SPEED OF EXECUTION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l05934}05934 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06023}06023   wdtol = epsilon(0.0\_dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06024}06024   wdtol = max(wdtol, 0.5d-\/18)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06025}06025   i1m = digits(0.0\_dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06026}06026   rln = log10( real( radix(0.0\_dp), kind=dp) ) * i1m}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06027}06027   fln = min(rln,20.0\_dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06028}06028   fln = max(fln,3.0\_dp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06029}06029   fln = fln -\/ 3.0\_dp}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06030}06030   zm = 1.8000\_dp + 0.3875\_dp * fln}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06031}06031   mz = zm + 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06032}06032   zmin = mz}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06033}06033   zdmy = z}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06034}06034   zinc = 0.0\_dp}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06035}06035   \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (z < zmin) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06036}06036     zinc = zmin -\/ nz}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06037}06037     zdmy = z + zinc}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06038}06038 \textcolor{keywordflow}{  END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06039}06039   zp = 1.0\_dp / zdmy}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06040}06040   t1 = cf(1) * zp}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06041}06041   s = t1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06042}06042   \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (zp >= wdtol) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06043}06043     zsq = zp * zp}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06044}06044     tst = t1 * wdtol}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06045}06045     \textcolor{keywordflow}{DO}  k = 2, 22}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06046}06046       zp = zp * zsq}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06047}06047       trm = cf(k) * zp}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06048}06048       \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (abs(trm) < tst) \textcolor{keywordflow}{EXIT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06049}06049       s = s + trm}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06050}06050 \textcolor{keywordflow}{    END DO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06051}06051 \textcolor{keywordflow}{  END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06052}06052 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06053}06053   \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (zinc == 0.0\_dp) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06054}06054     tlg = log(z)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06055}06055     fn\_val = z * (tlg-\/1.0\_dp) + 0.5\_dp * (con-\/tlg) + s}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06056}06056     \textcolor{keywordflow}{RETURN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06057}06057 \textcolor{keywordflow}{  END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06058}06058   zp = 1.0\_dp}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06059}06059   nz = zinc}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06060}06060   \textcolor{keywordflow}{DO}  i = 1, nz}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06061}06061     zp = zp * (z + (i-\/1))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06062}06062 \textcolor{keywordflow}{  END DO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06063}06063   tlg = log(zdmy)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06064}06064   fn\_val = zdmy * (tlg-\/1.0\_dp) -\/ log(zp) + 0.5\_dp * (con-\/tlg) + s}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06065}06065   \textcolor{keywordflow}{RETURN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cbessel_8f90_source_l06066}06066 \textcolor{keywordflow}{END IF}}
